The gun accidentally discharged, and Zhu was fatally shot. The merchant corps has captured Yu Decai and handed him over to the county government for legal action.

Jiangyin 69

Cheng Huirong Sentenced to Eleven Months in Prison: Cheng Huirong, a teacher at the Xiwai Jizhong Primary School, was reported by Xu Zhongchen, a self-confessed Communist Party member, as being the Minister of Organization of the County Tao Branch. The County Rectification Committee sent him to the county for interrogation. He was then transferred to the Suzhou High Court for further investigation. The case has now concluded, and he has been sentenced to eleven months in prison.

The Money Industry Convenes to Postpone Account Settlement: The money industry is the hub of finance. Last year, most firms were affected by bad debts. In addition, the Finance Bureau, facing local financial difficulties, frequently issued local public bonds by mortgaging supplementary taxes, which could not be repaid on schedule. The overall account settlement on February 16th was difficult to complete due to continuous rain and snow, leading to poor business conditions for all firms. Feng Taiyuan even conducted an account investigation. Yesterday (the 22nd), the Money Industry Association held a meeting and resolved that in the future, when bad debts occur, each firm should naturally handle the situation before any announcement is made. After an announcement is made, no further account adjustments or private settlements are allowed. Losses and difficulties should be shared fairly.

Since the major settlement period was hindered by rain and snow, each household that did not complete the settlement is considered excusable and should settle by the end of February. Before settlement is completed, no credit extension or continued dealings will be permitted. If a guarantor causes trouble or fails to fulfill their obligations, they will be considered to have violated their creditworthiness. Any firm or company established by the guarantor will not be allowed to conduct business with the other firms until the guarantor's obligations are fulfilled. A meeting is scheduled for March 1st to discuss related matters.

An Attempted Arson by Robbers: In Chen Nianqiao, Shuangpai Seventh Section, the home of Chen Jinchi had already been robbed once. The night before last, five robbers armed with pistols came again. Chen Jinchi only left women at home. The robbers demanded five hundred yuan, but the women refused. The robbers then set fire to rice straw, but fortunately, the fire did not spread to the house.

Danyang 70

Villagers in Hengtang Bridge Resist Arrest: Gambling has always been prevalent in Hengtang Bridge in the eastern township.

The Public Security Bureau specially dispatched Inspector Guo Shao, leading many police officers, to investigate and arrest gamblers. Eight gamblers and gambling equipment were captured at a teahouse. As they were preparing to take them to the city, a group of troublemakers incited the villagers to resist arrest. They forcibly took back the gamblers and gambling equipment and also seized two Browning pistols carried by police officers. Patrol officers Lin Shaobo and Tian Tongling were injured in the head. Inspector Guo has now returned to the city with the police officers and reported the incident to the county bureau for investigation.

The County Rectification Committee is Dismissed: Yang Duankai of the County Party Rectification Committee in this county left his post without approval. The Provincial Party Rectification Committee has discovered this and dismissed him from his position. Ju Yushu has been assigned to replace him in Danyang.

Zhenjiang 71

The Public Security Bureau Launches a Large-Scale Bandit Suppression Operation: The Provincial Public Security Bureau believes that bandits have recently been appearing in the Qiba and Badu areas, harming residents. Yesterday, it specially dispatched 400 police officers from the Police Brigade and Detective Squad, with 200 in plain clothes and 200 armed, to set out towards Gaozi Qiba and Badu respectively to suppress the bandits everywhere. As a result, they arrested several suspects, including Gao Daquan, Lu Yongcai, and Zhu Shaoquan.

The Banner People's Livelihood Institute Can Still Exist: Party member Chen Tianmin submitted a petition to the Provincial Relief Institute, accusing the Mongol Relief Institute of owning government property and requesting that it be run by the government. After verification by the institute in conjunction with the county government and with the approval of an internal order, it was determined that the term "Relief Institute" was misleading and should be changed to "Banner People's Livelihood Institute". The property belongs to the Banner People and should be managed by them.

Lu Disaster Refugees Seek Help from the Provincial Party Headquarters: Yesterday, 163 refugees, men and women, from Shanxian County, Shandong Province, arrived in the province from Taixing. Representatives Wang Xiusan and Zhang Guangyou went to the Provincial Party Headquarters at 3:00 PM with passports to seek assistance. The Party Headquarters, seeing their pitiful appearance, provided them with several silver dollars and instructed them to return to their hometown as soon as possible.

Yangzhou 72

Summary of Joint Bandit Suppression by Jiangsu and Anhui: Large gangs of bandits, numbering over a thousand, were discovered in Gaoyou Xiaojinggou and Tianwang counties, which border Jiangsu and Anhui provinces, in late January. The Superintendent's Office dispatched Zhao Brigade Han Tuanfu Zhengping, leading two battalions of soldiers, to advance to the vicinity of Tianchang and ordered Wang Brigade to send two battalions of soldiers to XInji Licheng, to jointly surround and suppress the bandits with Xu Tuan from Xuyu County, Anhui Province. The bandits fled west to the Laoheshan stronghold and the Changshan area of Shibali in Xiaoyushan. It is now reported that Xu Tuan's Tuanfu has led his team to track them down to Gucheng, annihilating many bandits. The 94th Brigade and the County Magistrate of Gaoyou have reported the bandit suppression situation to the Superintendent's Office.

Yangzhong 73

A Burning, Robbery, and Kidnapping Incident Occurs in Baziqiao: The wealthy Jin Quan family in Xiaoquegang, east of Baziqiao in this county, was suddenly attacked by a dozen local bandits the night before last. Jin was fortunate to have received advance warning and had already transported his silver, money, and jewelry elsewhere. When the bandits arrived and found nothing of value, they were furious and set fire to five of his tile houses, completely destroying more than two hundred dan of rice stored in the house. The bandits then went to Tiejianggang and robbed the He Dexing family. Dissatisfied with their loot, they kidnapped a twelve-year-old boy named Jiaqu. The whereabouts of the kidnapped boy are currently unknown. The victim dare not report the incident for fear of retaliation from the bandits, which shows the extent of the bandits' power.

Hangzhou 74

The Highway Bureau Continues to Borrow Funds from Merchants: The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau previously incurred arrears in construction materials and wages. At the beginning of this month, it mortgaged 100,000 yuan of construction bonds to the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank to borrow 80,000 yuan to pay these arrears. As the bureau's outstanding construction costs are still significant and difficult to clear, it recently submitted another report to the Construction Department to borrow 12,000 silver dollars from the Continental Bank by mortgaging construction bonds with a face value of 10,000 yuan and construction bonds with a face value of 10,000 yuan, and to borrow 27,000 yuan from the Zhejiang Savings Bank by mortgaging construction bonds with a face value of 45,000 yuan. Agreements have already been made to transfer the funds.

Statistics on Cooperative Enterprises in Various Counties: The Zhejiang Construction Department has compiled accurate statistics on the cooperative societies in various counties that have been approved for registration, up to the end of the 19th year of the Republic. There are a total of 410 cooperative societies with 11,686 members and a total share capital of 55,791 yuan. The distribution is as follows: Hangzhou City: 10 societies, 182 people, 687 yuan; Hang County: 78 societies, 2,159 people, 10,394 yuan; Haining: 31 societies, 738 people, 2,684 yuan; Fuyang: 28 societies, 1,260 people, 6,549 yuan; Yuhang: 28 societies, 778 people, 1,684 yuan; Lin'an: 7 societies, 121 people, 244 yuan; Jiaxing: 46 societies, 865 people, 4,192 yuan; Jiashan: 9 societies, 466 people, 239 yuan; Haiyan: 6 societies, 188 people, 290 yuan; Chongde: 53 societies, 882 people, 2,257 yuan; Wuxing: 8 societies, 404 people, 1,003 yuan; Changxing: 1 society, 22 people, 59 yuan; Deqing: 63 societies, 1,348 people, 5792 yuan; Wukang: 2 societies, 40 people, 36 yuan; Anji: 1 society, 16 people, 16 yuan; Yin County: 1 society, 18 people, 1,980 yuan; Shaoxing: 3 societies, 89 people, 9,460 yuan; Xiaoshan: 3 societies, 1221 people, 1,884 yuan; Zhuji: 3 societies, 172 people, 549 yuan; Yuyao: 2 societies, 247 people, 1062 yuan; Sheng County: 7 societies, 137 people, 685 yuan; Jinhua: 7 societies, 122 people, 444 yuan; Pujiang: 2 societies, 37 people, 120 yuan; Qu County: 3 societies, 37 people, 153 yuan; Yongjia: 4 societies, 117 people, 196 yuan; Suichang: 2 societies, 83 people, 764 yuan; Ruian: 2 societies, 53 people, 196 yuan.

Ningbo 75

Suspicion Remains After the Purser is Redeemed: The Xin Ningtai ship of the Ninghai Wheel Bureau was robbed by pirates outside Haimen Chuanjiao at the beginning of this month, and over ten people, including the ship's purser, Ying Tang, were kidnapped. It is now learned that the ship's comprador, Yu, withdrew 3,500 yuan from the company's surplus funds and redeemed Ying. However, suspicions about the comprador, Yu, regarding this robbery remain. It is said that when the robbery occurred, Yu remained calm and sat in his cabin without moving. The bandits looked around but did not ask him to identify Ying. Instead, they only threatened the shipowner to hand over the purser. Afterwards, the comprador, Yu, withdrew 3,500 yuan from the company's surplus funds and went to the bandits to redeem Ying. Considering the circumstances before and after the event, Yu is not without suspicion. It is reported that the ship company has filed a complaint with the authorities.

Meningitis Discovered in Yin County: An outbreak of meningitis has recently been discovered in the eastern townships of Yin County, and it is spreading rapidly. Yesterday (the 20th), the number of patients reached more than twenty in one day.

Robbers Loot a Nunnery: Shuimen Cave in the East Gate of Fenghua is a bustling area of Fengcheng. There is a nunnery there that has some property. At 9:00 PM on the 21st, seven or eight robbers suddenly arrived, each holding a pistol. They grabbed the abbess of the nunnery, Jing Shou, and forced her to reveal the location of the hidden silver. When she refused, they shot her in the head, causing severe injuries. The robbers then looted everything in the nunnery. By the time the military police arrived after hearing the alarm, the robbers had already fled without a trace.

Letter Received

Letter from Zhuang Zhengxiong, Fengxian 76

To the esteemed editor,

Having read the Fengxian local correspondence on page three of your esteemed newspaper on the fourteenth,

I was shocked to see my name, Zhengxiong, mentioned in the report regarding the Nantang River project case's court hearing. I am a guest from Wuxi and have no involvement with local affairs. I am entirely unrelated to the Nantang River project case. I am deeply concerned about being implicated and causing confusion. I hereby request a correction. Zhuang Zhengxiong from Fengxian, February 21st.

Special Item

Outline of Construction Projects in Shaanxi Province, Year 20 of the Republic of China (Continued) 77

▲Drafted by the Shaanxi Provincial Government

Third, Regarding Water Conservancy: The Jun'erzui Water Diversion Project has been undertaken by the Provincial Government in cooperation with the China International Famine Relief Commission, with a joint investment of 960,000 yuan. It is currently under construction. However, this project is a scaled-down plan. Once completed, it will irrigate one million mu of land and benefit parts of Jingyuan, Gao, and Lin counties. If the larger project of Zheng Bai's water diversion plan is implemented, combining the Jing, Zhi, Qing, Zhuo, and Qi rivers, it could restore the scale of Zheng Guo Canal, which irrigated 45,000 hectares of land. Of the eight million yuan in disaster relief bonds issued by the Central Government for Shaanxi, half is planned to be allocated to support the implementation of the larger project. The remaining funds will be supplemented by the profits generated after the success of this smaller project. Water conservancy projects in other areas will be supervised by the government, with counties raising funds to implement them. On the banks of the Wei River, ten kerosene-powered pumps will be purchased within this year to draw water for irrigation as a demonstration project for the people. Each pump will have four horsepower and cost 350 yuan including official expenses, totaling 3,500 yuan. Water level and flow stations will be established on the Wei River, Yellow River, Han River, and their major tributaries to serve as the basis for water conservancy calculations, requiring 300 yuan for surveys and 1,000 yuan for measurement costs. Fourth, Regarding Industry: The Shaanxi First Textile Factory will be established in Jiaokou Town, with 10,000 spindles, requiring approximately 1.5 million yuan. It will be jointly operated by the government and merchants. The preparations are actively underway, and the factory is expected to be established and open for operation in the 21st year of the Republic of China. The next project to be planned is a 5,000-spindle hydroelectric spinning mill in Jingyang Zhihe Town, requiring approximately 700,000 yuan. If these two factories are fully established, they can generate profits of over one million yuan annually. At the same time, the promotion of private household weaving will be even more beneficial. The cottonseeds discarded by the mill will be used to establish an oil extraction plant for utilization. There are three other industrial projects that should be prepared or researched and planned:

(A) Establishing a Xi'an Power Plant: The initial capacity of this plant is planned to be 500 kilowatts, requiring approximately 200,000 yuan. It is also planned to be jointly operated by the government and merchants, and preparations are underway. (To be continued)

Zhu Jiahua Sternly Warns Students of Central University Against Arrogance 78

▲Lalema Lectures at Central University on the Geography of Yunnan

Nanjing, 24th (Central News Agency): Zhu Jiahua, the president of Central University, sternly warned students against arrogance in a notice on the 24th due to poor order during the university's memorial week. Also, the German professor of geography, Lalema, from Sun Yat-sen University in Guangdong, went to Yunnan to investigate the geography and returned to Beijing. Zhu Jiahua invited him to give a lecture at Central University on the geography of Yunnan, the Pianma issue, and the work he has done since April, starting on the 24th for three consecutive days.

New Agricultural Facilities at the Jiangsu Provincial Agricultural Education Hall 79

The Jiangsu Provincial Agricultural Education Hall has recently added the following new agricultural facilities: (1) Expanding the experiment field: The hall has been promoting improved cotton and wheat varieties over the years, supplied by the College of Agriculture of Central University. However, due to the limited quantity, it has not been able to meet the needs of Tangshan, and relying on others is not a long-term solution. Therefore, it is planned to breed its own varieties. In addition to renting three mu of fertile land and thirteen mu of cultivated land, it has recently purchased seven and a half mu of cultivated land to prepare for the propagation and improvement of cotton and rice varieties. (2) Acquiring new agricultural implements: The hall has recently purchased a three-horsepower engine water pump, a rice thresher, and a cotton gin from the China New Agricultural Implements Promotion Association for trial use. Once successful, it will organize an irrigation cooperative to promote their use. (3) Promoting improved silkworm breeds and mulberry saplings: Last year, the hall produced 100 sheets of improved silkworm eggs to supply to students in the hall's silkworm and mulberry class and to farmers for breeding. Recently, it purchased a large number of mulberry saplings from Jinling University and distributed them to farmers for planting. With three to five years of effort from the hall, it will not be difficult to transform Tangshan into a sericulture area.

Jinan University Board of Directors Holds Inaugural Meeting 80

Nanjing, 24th: The Board of Directors of Jinan University held an inaugural meeting at Sun Ke's residence on the evening of the 23rd, followed by the first meeting. Zheng Hongnian was elected as chairman, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) The charter of the Board of Directors was amended and approved. (2) Sun Ke, Chen Lifu, and Zheng Hongnian were elected as standing directors. (3) Chen Lifu and Ma Zhaojun were appointed as auditors to audit the new budget for the 20th year of the Republic. After the audit is completed, Zheng Hongnian will submit it to the Ministry of Education. (4) The president will send letters to all directors in March, inviting them to visit the school for inspection.

Record of the China Art Academy Meeting in Beijing 81

The Second Painting and Calligraphy Exhibition of the China Art Academy on Qiqi Road in this city has been held in Shanghai, Wuxi, Suzhou, Changzhou, and other places, and has received much praise. The opening ceremony was held on the 8th of this month at the Qingnian Hall in Beijing. Despite the severe cold weather and snow depth of one foot, visitors were still very enthusiastic. Prominent figures such as Shangcun Riling, Lin Foxing of the Legislative Yuan, Zhang Jingwen of the Customs Administration, Xu Beihong of the Central University Art Institute, Li Yishi, Pan Yuliang, Shao Yuanchong, Zhang Mojun, Zhang Xiaocen, and Zhizhi came to view the exhibition in the snow. They were greatly impressed by the works of the school's professors Ma Qikuan, Zhang Shanzi, Zhang Daqian, Zheng Manqing, Zhang Hongbi, Wang Shizilou, and Lou Xinzhou, as well as the paintings and calligraphy of prominent figures in Shanghai. It was generally agreed that the Beijing art community's emphasis on Chinese art was unprecedented in the history of exhibitions. The lottery was drawn on the 15th, with Zhang Ji, a member of the National Government, and Lai Lian of the Central Party Headquarters serving as fair notaries. The meeting ended yesterday and returned to Shanghai.

Establishment of Branches by the Fisheries Society 82

▲Establishing Methods to Improve Society Affairs

The Fisheries Society of the Republic of China was established in August of the 15th year of the Republic. Its purpose is to unite comrades in the study of fisheries science, innovate fisheries enterprises, and improve fisheries material organizations in order to implement the Principle of People's Livelihood. In order to strengthen connections with comrades and promote the society's affairs, twelve methods to improve society affairs were established, and branches are being established in coastal provinces. Charter of the China Education Construction Society 84

Information about the organization of the China Education Construction Society by the domestic education sector has been reported previously. The following is the society's proposed charter: (1) Name: The name of this society is the China Education Construction Society. (2) Purpose: The purpose of this society is to unite comrades in education, study practical issues in education, and jointly promote the construction of education in China. (3) Membership: Anyone engaged in education or interested in educational construction, introduced by two members of the society, may become a member of the society. (4) Organization: (A) The society will initially establish three departments: General Affairs, Publications, and Communications. Each department will have one staff member, with the General Affairs staff member serving as the chairman, elected by all members. (B) When the society's affairs expand, branches may be established in various regions at home and abroad, with Shanghai as the address of the head office. The regulations for branches will be determined separately. (5) Duties: (A) The General Affairs staff member is responsible for managing documents, accounting, and convening meetings. (B) The Publications staff member is responsible for editing, publishing, and distributing publications. (C) The Communications staff member is responsible for investigation, introduction, and communication. (6) Work: (A) Research: Members must investigate and research certain educational issues and make systematic reports and discussions. (B) Collection: Members must collect new educational works from home and abroad. (C) Publication: A modern education journal will be published monthly, with contributions from members. (D) Society Development: Members must, in accordance with the society's purpose, connect with comrades in education and jointly promote the development of the society's affairs. (7) Term of Office: The term of office for each department's staff member is one year, and they may be re-elected. (8) Meetings: (A) General meetings of members will be held quarterly, with the General Affairs staff member determining the location and time and sending out a notice. If necessary, a special meeting may be convened at the request of one-third of the members. (B) Staff meetings will be held monthly, with the General Affairs staff member determining the location and time and sending out a notice. If there are other urgent matters, communication via letter may be used instead of a meeting. (9) Dues: (A) Admission fee: Each member must pay an admission fee of three yuan in national currency, payable in full at the time of admission. (B) Annual membership fee: Each member must pay an annual membership fee of one yuan in national currency. (C) Special fees: If necessary, a temporary decision may be made to collect special fees. (10) Supplementary Provisions: This charter will be implemented upon approval by the general meeting of all members. If there are any matters not covered, they may be submitted to the general meeting of members for resolution and amendment.

Tao Baichuan Officially Takes Office as Principal of the Municipal Jingye Middle School Yesterday 85

Tao Baichuan, a member of the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters, has been appointed as the principal of the Municipal Jingye Middle School by the Municipal Education Bureau, but he has repeatedly declined the position. All other teaching staff will continue in their positions. A meeting of all teaching staff will be convened in the coming days to discuss matters related to the development of the school.

Introduction to Senior and Junior High School Chinese-English Weekly 87

Results of Yesterday's Shanghai Basketball Association Matches 92

Yesterday's Shanghai Basketball Association matches consisted of four groups, with three matches in Group A. The most intense and interesting match was the last one between Huadong and Mailing. The results were: (1) Zhenru defeated Jianhua (Group A) 40-38; (2) Shangzhong defeated Youji (Group B) 52-18; (3) Chidui defeated Laoda (Group A) 39-23; (4) Huadong defeated Mailing (Group A) 37-29. A brief account of the Group A matches is as follows:

▲Zhenru defeated Jianhua: The performances of both sides were unremarkable. Zhenru led 22-12 in the first half. In the second half, Jianhua rallied and launched a sharp counterattack. Liu Guorong scored occasionally. Initially, Zhenru did not show weakness and the score difference was usually between four and ten points, with Zhenru in the lead. Later, Jianhua made a concerted effort and narrowed the score to 40-38, but time ran out and they lost to Zhenru by two points. The referee was Jiang Xiangqing. ▲Chidui defeated Laoda: After the opening, Laoda was immediately depressed. The score was once close at 11-13. Chizhi's long throws were very accurate, and soon the score was higher than Laoda. The first half ended 23-13. The situation in the second half was also unremarkable. As a result, Chidui scored 39 points and Laoda scored 23 points. The referee was Jiang Xiangqing.

▲Huadong defeated Mailing: This battle was very exciting, and the spectators were very excited. Under the mobilization, Wang Jinping of Huadong scored the first point, and Qian Jingdu and Yong also scored a goal, taking a 4-1 lead. Mailing tried hard to counterattack, and Henry and Shattai each scored, while Bei Pu made it 6-6. Brown scored a goal, surpassing Huadong with 8-6. The situation between the two sides was very fierce. Lu Zhongen made it 9-8. Since then, Mailing has been in the lead, with Huadong closely following behind. After fighting to 16-16, Henry of Mailing made a free throw, winning the first half with 17-16. At the beginning of the second half, Meng Zhi of Mailing scored first. Huadong fought cautiously, and Lu Zhongen made a great contribution. The score jumped to the lead from then on. Qian Jingyong, Ouyang, and Lu Zhongen all made contributions. Although Mai Neng tried hard to retaliate, he failed to catch up. As a result, Huadong won with 37-29. The referee was Zhang Guoxun.

The Jinan Football Zhenru Basketball Team's Philippine Campaign (13) 95

(Reported by our reporter Wen Chu from Manila on February 13)

▲The Football Team's Seventh Battle...Suffered a Crushing Defeat to the Lasa Team with a Score of 3-0

The Jinan University's ever-victorious army, which had won five games and drawn one in six battles, had fully intended to fight the Lasa team again after drawing with them in the final, to crush this strong enemy and complete the feat. Who would have expected it to be beyond our expectations? Moreover, the situation of their defeat was also unexpected by the general audience. This letter may arrive in Shanghai on the same day as the athletes. I am very unwilling to convey this unfortunate news to the eyes of the readers, so as to reduce the joy of the welcomers, but for the sake of detailed records, it cannot be omitted. Moreover, defeat is a common occurrence in military affairs. After this lesson, or one more experience, then this setback may be the accumulation of a great success in the future. If so, then although I am unwilling to write about this tragic defeat, its situation is worth recording.

▲The Enemy Was Determined to Win

Since the first battle resulted in a draw, our army won all four subsequent battles. The enemy team officials visited the site for every match and discussed our strengths and weaknesses, and who was the strongest player. They deeply expected that there would be continued competition after the five games, so they continued to train every day. After the date of the rematch was confirmed, they even organized a cheering squad to cheer and strengthen the morale of the army. Therefore, the school invested in purchasing 500 half-price tickets and distributed them to students to attend and cheer. Before the match, the cheering squad made noises, blew trumpets and drums, and sang songs of victory to disrupt our army's mind. With a lone army expedition, it is normal to occasionally suffer setbacks after being exhausted. Moreover, their great achievements are still there, right?

▲The Enemy Opened the Record in Three Minutes

The game started at 3:00 PM on the 13th. After selecting the door to take photos in the first half, George O'Brien, a movie star from the American Fox Company traveling to the Philippines, was specially invited to kick off the ball, and the battle began. Our forwards advanced with the ball. When they reached the center, the enemy general blocked the ball, and the ball was uncertain in the center. The two sides were trying to mediate. The enemy's left inside forward suddenly went forward with the ball and shot at our goal from more than ten yards away. Xie Quanhe failed to protect it, and the cheerleaders in the audience cheered wildly for their victory.

▲Our Army's Counterattack Was Ineffective

Although our side lost this goal, we tried hard to counterattack. Once, Luo Jiajiang shot fiercely at the enemy from the rear, but was kicked by the goalkeeper. General Hei rushed up and added a kick, but was also kicked out. It can be said that these two balls had a chance to enter the city, but their iron city gate was still the General Chuan who defended Zhuozhou City the other day.

▲Xie Quanhe's Contribution Was Indelible

After being pressed twice by the enemy, because they had already gained the upper hand, they showed their long-distance skills and approached our side three times in a row, aiming at the city gate and firing three shots. All of them were saved by this newly appointed garrison envoy General Xie. Even the other side applauded and praised him. Not long after, Jiang Shanjing was knocked down by the enemy's forward when he bravely resisted the enemy. He was fined a penalty kick, but was also saved by General Xie kneeling on the ground. His contribution was truly indelible.

▲Unfortunately, Another Good Opportunity Was Lost

Center Dai took advantage of Xie Quanhe's kicked out ball and ran forward, passing the forward line and passing it to Chen Bingxiang, the ambushing army on the right. Chen took it to the left corner of the play gate and shot it temporarily because it was too high and did not enter the net. Our side forced a corner kick from this, and Mei Hongbao picked it up and sent it. The landing point was directly opposite the enemy's gate, and was punched out by the goalkeeper, which really made the overseas Chinese audience sigh.

▲They Were Lucky and We Were Unlucky

The two sides fought fiercely again. The other side got a corner kick opportunity, which was kicked by their right wing. The right inside forward was waiting for the opportunity to hit the person with his head, and it became 2-0. When the first half was about to end, General Hei got a rear pass and drove straight in. He shot fiercely to the right more than ten yards away. At this time, the enemy goalkeeper was also unable to catch it, but the ball hit the goal post and turned outward. Mei Hongbao rushed to it and was rescued by the enemy, and the first half ended.

▲Three Goals All Missed Opportunities

After the break, we changed places to fight again. Our side tried our best to fight back and wanted to regain the lost ground. Therefore, Generals Feng and Jiang, who guarded the two cities, both ventured to cross the enemy's territory and prepared to charge. Once, Center Dai and General Hei were sent a ball from the rear, and the two generals passed it to each other and advanced at the same time, breaking through the barrier straight in, which was a matter of time, but was stopped by the enemy's iron goalkeeper. Center Dai intercepted the kicked out ball and passed it to General Hei again. General Hei passed it to Fu Hexuan. When Fu kicked, it was kicked out by the iron goalkeeper again. General Hei took advantage of the situation to exert his strength again, and the ball entered the net. The referee judged it to be offside and canceled it. This was an unfortunate event. After a short period of melee, Center Dai kicked another ball in from the left, and at the same time was knocked down by the enemy's rear forward, injuring his face. The referee judged that the kicked in ball was invalid due to offside. This was the second unfortunate event. Also, because the enemy rushed in with great force, a penalty kick was awarded. Center Dai took the kick, but because he was too anxious to make a contribution, it was too high and crossed the net. This was the third unfortunate event. When the reporter saw this, his hands and feet were almost cold, just like when Mr. Zhuge set fire to Hulu Valley, Sima Yi and his sons were all seriously injured and waiting to die. But heaven did not bless the Han Dynasty, and electric rain fell, causing the Sima family and his sons to return safely. When reading The Romance of the Three Kingdoms to this point, everyone abandoned the book and sighed three times. On that day, many people were angry and left the stadium when they saw the two goals had entered and were judged invalid, and one penalty kick did not fall into the net.

▲The Dust of the Expedition Rolled On, But Ultimately to No Avail

Since our side lost these three goal opportunities, although the five tigers in the front and the three fierce players in the center worked hard to gallop and hoped to save the situation, in the 25 minutes of the second half, almost 30 minutes were spent launching a general attack in the enemy's territory. However, since their hearts were flustered, the ball was not accurate, and the opportunities to get corner kicks and shoot at the center were either too high or too off. It was truly a case of six expeditions to Qishan without gaining an inch of land, making the athletes work hard to no avail, and the audience sighing. What a pity, what a pity.

▲Lost Opportunity Again When the Game Was About to End

When the entire army was far out, the rear was empty, which was very dangerous in terms of defense. Sure enough, five or six minutes before the end of the game, the enemy's forward got the ball and attacked from the right. There was no time to rush to the rescue, and another goal was scored. Therefore, a crushing defeat was announced with a score of 3-0.

▲Victory Cannot Be Relied On, Relying On It Will Surely Lead to Defeat

Since a lone army was sent out on a series of victories, it must have had special skills to be able to achieve this. However, just like Napoleon, who swept across Europe with great power, ultimately failed in Russia. Relying on victory and being proud is also like Ruo Ao in the Spring and Autumn period being complacent in the battle of Pusao. During the welcome night of the advisory group, I heard a player talk about his battle achievements, and when he mentioned the Lasa team, he said that because he did not know the enemy's situation and everything else when he first arrived, he drew with them. After that, winning was just a matter of raising his foot. Although this cannot represent the psychology of all the players, if most people believe that they will win, then they will inevitably underestimate the enemy. Moreover, after a ceasefire of more than ten days, there was no suitable field to practice on. Compared to the enemy's continuous training, it was also a factor in the failure. Because of this defeat, a better way to control the enemy was formulated. This failure has benefited me a lot.

▲Popular Opinion Follows After Success

The overseas Chinese public, who did not understand the details of the rematch, almost all opposed this competition. The greatest reason was that five wins and one draw could be said to be a perfect record. It would have been a great joy to return with this reputation. Therefore, since the news of the continued competition came out, the youth association dormitory has been filled with criticism, hearing dozens of cases every day. Therefore, the audience on that day was also a very small number in the overseas Chinese community, and the athletes' courage to move forward seemed to be lessened as a result. By analogy, if a person owns a large army to claim hegemony, but loses popular opinion, it is appropriate for him not to be able to succeed.

Shanghai County Prepares for People's Congress Election 96

▲Order from the Provincial Government Stipulating the Schedule for Preparing for the Election

Yan Shenyu, the county magistrate of Shanghai County, received Commission Order No. 126 from Hu Pu'an, the Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs and concurrently the Chief Supervisor of the Jiangsu Election for the National Assembly Representative, yesterday. The order stated that Yan Shenyu was appointed as the Shanghai Election Supervisor for the National Assembly Representative. In addition, a telegram was received, stipulating the schedule for preparing for the election in various places. The text stated, "Shanghai County National Assembly Representative Election Supervisor, please read. Regarding the National Assembly's election office's telegram, the date for the National Assembly meeting was originally set for May 5th. Now that the meeting date is not far away, the preparation for the election in various places should be completed before April 20th. The following schedule for preparing for the election in various places is now stipulated. Each election supervisor or election supervisor should immediately follow the provisions of the National Assembly Representative Election Law and its implementation regulations, and earnestly handle the following matters, and estimate the date distribution as follows: (1) Each local election supervisor should notify various local groups to prepare detailed registers and submit them for review, estimating the time required to be seven days. (2) The election supervisor should immediately submit these registers to the election supervisor for review and determine the election qualifications of their groups and members, estimating the time required to be ten days. (3) After the election qualifications of each group have been determined, the election supervisor will prepare the general register of voters by occupation in the local area and the register of voters for the group, and send them to each election supervisor for public announcement, estimating the time required to be ten days. (4) After the register is announced, if the individual believes that there are errors or omissions, he may, within five days after the announcement, present evidence and request the election supervisor to forward it to the election supervisor for verification, estimating the time required to be five days. (5) After the election supervisor in each locality announces the register, he should immediately announce a scheduled voting election, estimating the time required to be three days. (6) After the voting is over, the ballots should be counted immediately. After the ballots are counted, the ballot counting administrator should prepare the ballot counting record, and immediately prepare a report on the ballot counting situation and send it to the election supervisor, estimating three days. (7) The election supervisor should prepare a report after the election of each group in his jurisdiction, send it along with various documents to the election supervisor, and announce the election situation of each group in his jurisdiction, estimating seven days (8) The election supervisor will collect various election documents, calculate the number of votes for each candidate, verify the number of elected representatives, announce the elected representatives, and notify the elected persons, estimating the time required to be five days. (9) After receiving the notification, the elected person should indicate in writing within ten days whether or not he wishes to be elected, estimating ten days. (10) The election supervisor will issue the certificate of election and travel expenses to the elected person, estimating one day. The above is a total estimate of 61 days. (11) The elected representatives will set off to Beijing to report, depending on the distance from the capital. The date on the right is attached, but it is only to show the standard for the preparation of the election. The circumstances in various places are different, and may be increased or decreased depending on the convenience of transportation. The election must be completed as scheduled so that the elected representatives can report to Beijing in early May. You should follow the instructions carefully, and if there is any delay in the election, you will be severely punished. Be sure to follow the instructions." The seal of Hu Pu'an, Chief Supervisor of the Jiangsu Election for the National Assembly Representative, was counted and the date list of county affairs that should be handled in the election of each county was attached (omitted).

Revised Closing Date 97

▲The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Seeks Opinions

Yesterday, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to the Federation of Provincial Chambers of Commerce and a letter to various industry associations in the city, saying, "Dear Sirs, on the 19th of this month, Mr. Wang Yansong, a standing committee member of the Chamber of Commerce, proposed the following: 'Regarding the deadline for settlement in the business community, the Chamber of Commerce previously considered that the end of the lunar year was inconvenient for both farmers and merchants, and proposed to change the date of the total settlement and collection to the day before the beginning of spring. However, since the beginning of spring is on February 4th or 5th every year, it is still not very convenient to settle in the middle of the year. If the national calendar is still calculated based on the end of the lunar year every year, it will not only make the year indefinite and difficult to calculate, but it will also be greatly contrary to the central government's intention to promote the national calendar. Recalling the state of panic and doubt in the business community when the deadline for collection in the 19th year had not been determined, and the suspension of commerce, the settlement date in the 20th year should be discussed in advance to avoid digging a well when you are thirsty. Yansong read in the newspaper that the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau submitted a document to the mayor, proposing that from the 20th year onwards, the fiscal year for national industry and commerce should be changed to start from March 1st of this year to the end of February of the following year. The first settlement and collection period each year is at the end of June, the second is at the end of October, and the third total settlement and collection period is at the end of February of the following year. This is in line with both government orders and commercial conditions. The Chamber of Commerce should separately telegraph the municipal government and the Executive Yuan to express its approval so that a decision can be made as soon as possible. Is this appropriate? Please decide publicly.' The matter was brought up for discussion at the 12th Standing Committee meeting of the Executive Committee of the Chamber of Commerce on the 20th of this month, and it was resolved to send letters to various industry associations to solicit opinions, limiting them to reply to the meeting within two weeks, and also to send letters to various provincial chambers of commerce to solicit opinions. Therefore, we are sending this letter to inquire about your opinions on the above-mentioned revised closing date method. Please express your valuable opinions at any time so that the official authorities can adopt them. This would be greatly appreciated."

Yangtze River Six Companies Implement Business Alliance 100

▲ Open Cooperation in Freight Transportation

▲ Subsidizing Weaker Shipping Companies

Shipping companies on all routes are gradually moving towards cooperation. Since the four companies on the Shanghai-Ningbo line implemented the alliance last year, business has flourished and revenue has increased significantly. This year, the alliance will continue, but the method will be slightly changed. The original plan of allocating 80% of the revenue among the four companies will be changed to 41% this year. Ning Shao will receive 11%, and Butterfield & Swire, Sanpei, and China Merchants will each receive 10%. Subsequently, the six ships on the Shanghai-Taiwan route will also follow this method for joint operation, which will not only eliminate business disputes but also significantly increase freight income. It is noted that the number of operators on the Yangtze River route has been increasing in recent years, and the number of ships has also increased. Butterfield & Swire, Jardine Matheson, Nisshin Kisen Kaisha, China Merchants, Sanpei, Ning Shao, and other six companies have always had a freight association, but it was only in name and not in reality. Freight rates were inconsistent, causing losses to the companies. Now, the six companies have also formed a large-scale alliance for cooperation on the Yangtze River route. A meeting was held yesterday to discuss the details of this matter, as detailed below.

▲ Butterfield & Swire's Proposal: Butterfield & Swire has the most ships on the Yangtze River. Recently, seeing that the freight alliance has been ineffective and various companies have been excessively discounting freight rates, which benefits passengers, it has become difficult for Yangtze River ships to maintain operations. Therefore, it was proposed to move from a freight alliance to a business alliance, following the Ningbo route model. The six companies will implement an open business alliance, and this idea was solicited from the other five companies. As a result, Jardine Matheson, Nisshin Kisen Kaisha, China Merchants, Sanpei, and Ning Shao all expressed their support. Therefore, representatives from each company were invited to Butterfield & Swire yesterday for the first discussion meeting.

▲ Consultation Method: Yesterday, responsible representatives from each of the six companies went to Butterfield & Swire to discuss the cooperation method of the Yangtze River business alliance. First, the representative from Butterfield & Swire stated the benefits of cooperation and the dangers of not uniting. Then, the proposed cooperation method was presented. Generally, Yangtze River business will be allocated according to the number of ships and schedules of the six companies. Small companies with fewer ships will be given assistance. For example, if the old Ning Shao ship can load 1,000 tons of cargo but only loads 500 tons, the other five companies will jointly subsidize 250 tons to avoid losses. After implementation, each ship's export cargo manifest will be exchanged for review, either monthly or quarterly. Detailed methods will be decided at the second general meeting.

▲ Representatives' Opinions: This alliance business is unprecedented on the Yangtze River and will be implemented for at least one year. After implementation, freight rates will not be excessively reduced, and passengers will pay according to the price, without any reduction in transportation volume. Recovering hidden losses will be most cost-effective for the shipping companies. The representative from Nisshin Kisen Kaisha suggested that the term need not be fixed and could be dissolved at any time. The discussion resulted in an initial term of nine months. Whether to continue after nine months will be decided within these three months. The representative from China Merchants proposed that special subsidies should be given to companies with fewer ships, which was met with sympathy.

▲ External Shipping Companies: In addition to the six companies, there are also British-owned Jardine Matheson, American-owned Yangtze Rapid Steamship Co., Chinese-owned Zhaoxing, and Nanhua shipping companies on the Yangtze River line, as well as so-called "wild chicken" Yangtze River ships. At that time, the representatives proposed whether to invite them to join the alliance. As a result, it was decided that the above shipping companies did not have regular Yangtze River ships, and the total number of ships was less than one-third of the six companies, so there was no obstacle to the alliance business. Therefore, it was not necessary to ask them to join. The meeting was adjourned immediately after the discussion.

▲ Freight Issue: After the price increase, each ship suffered huge hidden losses.

Yangtze River freight rates had already increased by 15% before the shallow water season and another 15% during the shallow water season. According to the usual practice, the shallow water fee should be abolished on March 1. Now, the representatives proposed that after the alliance, this shallow water fee should not be canceled and another 15% should be added. The Sichuan route will increase by 30% of the original amount. This issue will be decided at the second meeting when the alliance method is implemented.

Prohibition of Ordinary Shops Operating Savings 102

▲ Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Orders Closure Within One Month

The Municipal Government previously requested instructions from the Ministry of Finance to prohibit ordinary shops from operating savings. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau was ordered to strictly prohibit this. It is reported that the bureau has now ordered all such companies to immediately stop collecting funds and refund savings, with a deadline for closure within one month. The full text is as follows: Order to comply with the matter. Repeatedly received orders from the Municipal Government based on previous inquiries from the Ministry of Finance, stating that the China Innerwear Weaving Factory, Xinxin Department Store, Taidong Bookstore, and the Women's Virtue Savings Department jointly established by the Chinese and French Chinese and Western Pharmacies are all ordinary shops operating savings and should be prohibited. Furthermore, it was recently reported in the newspapers that the Shanghai Oriental Savings Association issued a notice of savings awards, and the Youhua Silver Company is preparing for full funding and revealing advertisements on the second day of each month, and the Shanghai Tongchang Car Company is handling savings car purchase department credit savings department and other items, all of which are illegal operations and should be strictly prohibited to prevent future troubles and uphold the law. Although Sincere and Wing On companies are registered with the Hong Kong government, the companies were originally organized with Chinese investment. Now that they have established companies in Shanghai, they should abide by Chinese laws and regulations and cannot disregard the law just because they are registered in Hong Kong. Therefore, we are instructed to comply with and handle and report separately. I hereby order that commercial establishments operating savings are illegal operations with many malpractices. This bureau is separately prohibiting them. The establishment of companies should especially strictly abide by the Provisional Rules for Company Registration and submit them to the competent authorities for registration for future reference. In accordance with the previous order, in addition to separately ordering compliance, you are hereby ordered to immediately stop collecting funds for the savings department you are operating and return the savings of each household within one month. The details of the closure should be reported for verification and transfer within ten days of the arrival of this document. Those companies that have not been registered in accordance with the regulations should also promptly apply for registration. This matter concerns the prohibition order and must not be regarded as a mere formality, lest it cause inconvenience. This order is imperative.

Rockefeller Agrees to Donate Funds for Chinese General Hospital 103

▲ Managed by Chinese After Completion

The Continental Daily reports that the sports field of the Chinese Athletic Advancement Association on Route Pére Robert in the French Concession is owned by the American oil magnate Rockefeller, covering approximately one hundred acres. Rockefeller has now agreed to allocate funds to build a hospital specifically for Chinese patients and has pledged to donate 2 million yuan for construction. However, this will only be allocated after the Chinese side has raised 2 million yuan on its own. According to this initiative, the local gentry and merchants have long felt the lack of a well-equipped modern hospital specifically for Chinese patients. When the lease agreement between the Athletic Advancement Association and the Rockefeller Foundation expired, the field was deemed the most suitable location for building a hospital. Therefore, Liu Ruiheng, Kong Xiangxi, Sun Ke, and others were elected to form a committee to contact the Rockefeller Foundation in New York. A telegram has been received from the United States stating that they have generously agreed and that Rockefeller will donate half of the construction costs. The remaining half is planned to be raised from the public to accumulate a large sum. Furthermore, one unique aspect of this initiative is that the architectural design and post-completion management will be entirely managed by Chinese.

Anti-Opium Society Requests Burning of Customs Opium 105

▲ Anti-Smuggling Committee Replies that it has Inquired and Handled

In November of last year, the Shanghai Jianghai Customs seized a large quantity of opium, totaling 19,400 pounds, on the German cargo ship Klopstock. Because the opium was being smuggled by the Japanese, the Japanese authorities made great efforts to release it, claiming it was being transported to Dalian. This opium is still held at the Jianghai Customs and no measures have been taken. The Chinese National Anti-Opium Society has sent a letter to the Central Anti-Smuggling Committee, requesting it to inquire with the Customs to burn the opium in order to show China's determination to ban opium. Yesterday, the Central Anti-Smuggling Committee replied, stating that the letter concerning the seizure of a large quantity of opium on a German cargo ship by the Jianghai Customs in November of last year had been forwarded to the Ministry of Finance, ordering the Customs to burn it in advance. However, no reply has been received, so they are urged to expedite the matter. It has been decided by the 74th Committee Meeting of the Committee to inquire with the Ministry of Finance again, ordering the Jianghai Customs to comply and burn it in advance. In addition to forwarding the case as is, a corresponding reply is hereby issued. Please investigate and comply. Sincerely, Chinese National Anti-Opium Society.

Ministry of Industry Convenes Conference on Silkworm Seed Inspection in Shanghai 106

Imported foreign silkworm seeds were previously inspected by personnel from the Silkworm Seed Inspection Office of the former Ministry of Agriculture and Mining. The office has now been ordered to merge with the Silk Inspection Department of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau. In the future, the import of foreign silkworm seeds will still need to be reported to the bureau for inspection and certification before being allowed to enter the country. The Ministry of Industry believes that the issue of silkworm seed inspection is of great importance to China's silk industry and experts should be convened for joint discussion. Therefore, Xu Tinghu, Director of the Agricultural Department, and Zou Bingwen, Director of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, have requested the agricultural administrative authorities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui provinces, as well as silkworm schools and institutions, to send representatives to a meeting at the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau at 10:00 AM on the 23rd of this month. Xu Tinghu, Director of the Ministry of Industry, He Yushu, Director of the Jiangsu Department of Agriculture and Mining, Wang Jiaxian, representative of the Zhejiang Construction Department, Shao Shenpei of the Jiangsu Women's Sericulture School, He Shangping of the International United Sericulture Improvement Association, Wu Huanru of the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Deng Ronghui of the Nanjing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Cai Wuji, Miao Zhongxiu, and Li An of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau attended. Xu Tinghu presided over the meeting and began with a speech, stating that China's silk exports have been sluggish in recent years, especially last year. Remedial measures can be divided into fundamental and symptomatic aspects. The symptomatic approach is to issue public bonds for relief. The fundamental aspect is the silkworm seed issue. The quality of silkworm seeds directly affects the quality and quantity of silk. In recent years, the improvement of silkworm seeds has been very successful, gaining the trust of farmers. However, speculators have taken advantage of this to mix inferior seeds under the guise of improved silkworm seeds, which is extremely harmful. In order to fundamentally remedy this situation, regulations on silkworm seed management will be proposed to the Ministry in the future. Subsequently, He Yushu, Director of the Jiangsu Department of Agriculture and Mining, reported on the progress of managing silkworm seed in Jiangsu Province over the past year, stating that silkworm seed inspection is necessary due to various reasons, but in reality, there are also various difficulties. The issue is complex and not just a matter for any one party. He provided detailed facts to prove this. Next, Miao Zhongxiu and Li An, Director and Deputy Director of the Silk Inspection Department of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, successively reported on the bureau's handling of silkworm seed inspection since taking over, and discussed the inspection methods and standards. Afterwards, various experts expressed their opinions. At 12:00, after a luncheon at the Bankers Association, the meeting resumed at 1:30 and the contents of the silkworm seed management regulations were discussed in detail. After the meeting ended at 4:00, Cai, Deputy Director of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, and Miao, Director of the Silk Inspection Department, led the participants to visit various departments of the bureau before dispersing.

Two Proposals from the National Coal Production and Sales Association 107

▲ Reduce National Coal Transportation Costs

▲ Designate Vehicles for Joint Transportation

The Ministry of Railways believes that transportation has gradually recovered in recent years and has decided to convene a National Commercial Transportation Conference in Beijing on March 1, inviting commercial associations, financial institutions, transportation companies, and other industries from across the country to discuss the development of railway services and the rectification of all matters. The National Coal Production and Sales Association of the Republic of China has been approved to send representatives to attend. The proposals of the association are recorded below.

▲ Telegram of Representatives' Names: To the Ministry of Railways in Nanjing. Regarding the Ministry's letter approving the association to send representatives to attend the National Commercial Transportation Conference, the association has designated Fang Jiaobo as the attending representative and Yu Shunqing as the observer representative. Two proposals are submitted, along with the names of the representatives, and telegraphed to the Ministry for approval and discussion. The Chairman of the National Coal Production and Sales Association of the Republic of China, Lin Kanghou, Standing Committee Members Fang Jiaobo, Hong Yanbin, Sheng Pihua, and Liu Yumen, respectfully.

▲ Proposal 1: Request to reduce national coal transportation costs and issue a general order to all routes to eliminate extortionate fees outside of transportation costs. (Reason) The price of coal in China often differs greatly between the mining company and the user, with the difference being several times the price. While there are considerable profits for coal merchants and commissions for intermediaries, transportation costs account for almost half of the coal price. Although national coal transportation costs are already classified as sixth class, it is still necessary to request a special reduction during this period of national coal decline. Moreover, during the era of warlord separatism, individuals withheld vehicles and extorted supplies from coal merchants who requested to borrow vehicles to transport coal. The amount often exceeded the transportation costs. Coal merchants had no choice but to pay with great pain. Now that the country is unified and the warlords have been eliminated, this type of extortion has largely become a precedent that has not been abolished, resulting in additional burdens on coal merchants. The cost is high and the selling price is high, making it impossible to compete with foreign coal. This is also a major reason why national coal cannot develop. It is proposed to the general meeting for discussion and resolution. (Method) Request the Ministry of Railways to reduce national coal transportation costs to show its support, and present a decree to the National Government ordering all routes, military police, and other departments not to extort extra fees, thereby increasing the cost of national coal and making it impossible to compete with foreign coal.

▲ Proposal 2: Request to issue a general order to all routes to designate vehicles for joint transportation of national coal. (Reason) The inability to develop national coal in China is due to various reasons, but transportation inconvenience is the biggest obstacle. It goes without saying that some areas are located in remote areas and are not connected by railways. Even mines along the railways also feel the difficulty of transportation. It is sometimes congested and sometimes clear, and cannot be fully transported. There are even cases where not a single vehicle can be obtained for years, resulting in a surplus of supply and a shortage of demand. Suppliers have mountains of coal that cannot be transported. The accumulation of coal poses a risk of burning, and miners are concerned about their livelihoods. Mine owners are sitting on their capital, often leading to failure. Demanders originally use national coal, but if it is available, the price may not be cheaper than foreign coal. If it is in short supply, foreign coal takes the opportunity to increase prices, resulting in losses. The losses of both parties are due to transportation inconvenience. It is proposed to the general meeting for discussion and resolution. (Method) Request the Ministry of Railways to issue a general order to all routes to estimate the amount of coal produced by each mine, designate a number of vehicles specifically for coal transportation, and not to be used for other purposes at any time. It also orders connecting routes to jointly transport coal to avoid interruption in the middle and to facilitate the smooth sale of national coal.

Second Meeting of the Business Tax Research Association 108

▲ Decides on Principles for Implementing Business Tax in This City

The Business Tax Research Committee organized by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce held its second committee meeting at 1:00 PM yesterday. Wang Yansong was elected as chairman and the meeting proceeded with formalities. First, Yan Egsheng reported on the previous resolution and the full text of the review committee's report. Then, according to the simplified rules of the subcommittee, Wang Yansong was elected as the chairman of this committee. Then, the full text of the review report was discussed. The principles for implementing business tax in this city are: (1) Except for luxury businesses, the tax rate should be the same and not exceed 0.2%; (2) It is better to have a low tax rate and widespread collection than a high tax rate that is difficult to implement; (3) Collection methods should be simple and avoid harassment. It is heard that all review reports have been passed by the committee meeting and submitted to the Standing Committee for discussion. They will then be submitted to the representative of the Municipal Finance Bureau as a basis for implementation.

Silk and Satin Industry Requests Exemption from Business Tax for Whole Sale Industry 109

▲ Telegrams to the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance

Yesterday, the Shanghai Silk and Satin Trade Association sent a telegram to the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing regarding the exemption of all silk and satin industries from business tax, stating: "The case of the silk and satin industry requesting a reduction in the business tax rate was previously submitted by the Ministry of Industry to the Executive Yuan and approved, ordering all provinces and cities not to exceed 0.2%, which shows the utmost concern for maintaining people's livelihoods and promoting domestic products. We are deeply impressed and grateful. It is especially beneficial to the silk merchants and the future of sericulture. We would like to further state that if the silk and satin factories have already had central government special taxes levied, all manufacturing industries and their directly established whole sale industries can be exempted from business tax, as clearly instructed in the Ministry of Finance's telegram reply to the association. This is because manufacturing industries are already burdened with special taxes and cannot be required to pay business tax again, causing double taxation. The scope of manufacturing industries naturally includes large-scale silk factories and small-scale handicraft workshops. In terms of nature, both are manufacturing. In terms of ability, small-scale workshops are weaker than factories. In terms of products, both those produced by workshops and those produced by factories should bear the same special taxes. Whole sale industries directly established by silk factories can be exempted from business tax. Whole sale issuance centers jointly entrusted by small-scale workshops, commonly known as silk shops, should also be exempted. As for the so-called 'merchants' in commerce, they are more like managers, only responsible for receiving and paying and not for profit. Although they seem to have the name of a business, they do not have its organization. The handling fees they earn may not even reach 0.01%, and the goods they handle have already been taxed with special taxes. In terms of tax laws and abilities, they are not able to bear business tax. We sincerely request the Ministry to issue a clear instruction so that we can follow it and avoid double taxation. The Shanghai Silk and Satin Trade Association respectfully."

Ministry Order to Revise Tax Rate for Paint and Rosewood Industry 110

The Shanghai Paint Industry Trade Association stated that the business tax regulations of Jiangsu Province stipulate excessively high tax rates for the paint, rosewood, and Western-style furniture industries, making it difficult to bear. Rosewood utensils and Western-style furniture are necessary household items, but they are regarded as luxury goods, which is not in line with the intention of maintaining people's livelihoods and promoting craftsmanship. The paint and furniture industries have repeatedly convened meetings. Based on the standard of no more than 0.2% as stipulated in Article 4 of the Ministry's outline, they have requested various industry trade associations and tax regulations research committees to send representatives with written statements to Beijing to petition for a reduction in the tax rate. The heads of various departments of the National Government agreed to adopt the proposal as much as possible and requested the Ministry of Finance to verify and handle the matter based on the situation. The Ministry of Finance's reply is as follows: "To the Shanghai Paint Industry Trade Association, we have read your telegram. The draft of the Jiangsu Business Tax Regulations has been submitted to the Ministry by the provincial government. The tax rate for the paint and rosewood industry should be revised separately and the provincial government should be consulted for implementation. Please be informed, signed Ministry of Finance."

Zhang Wenyi's Corpse Has Traces of Dissection 111

▲ Reported to Deng Zhenquan for Investigation

Zhang Wenyi, a 25-year-old native of Nantong and battalion commander of the garrison camp of the Wusong Fortress Command, suffered a ruptured blood vessel in his nose a few days ago, causing profuse bleeding. He was escorted to the Baolong Hospital on Baker Road in this city by an aide from the fortress command. After arriving at the hospital, doctors performed a hemostatic operation and the bleeding stopped. His condition was very good. Unexpectedly, Commander Zhang's health weakened due to excessive blood loss. On the morning of the 22nd of this month, his condition suddenly deteriorated and he passed away at around 1:00 PM in the afternoon. Since Commander Zhang's family was far away in Nantong, the fortress command urgently telegraphed his family to come to Shanghai. An aide was sent to the hospital to make arrangements to place Zhang's body in the hospital's mortuary for his family to claim. After Zhang's family received the telegram, his brother and a relative traveled to Shanghai by boat from Tongzhou and arrived on the previous day. Personnel from the fortress command accompanied them to purchase a coffin and went to Baolong Hospital for the funeral. When the hospital attendant opened the mortuary, the corpse was not in the mortuary. After inquiries, it was found in the dissection room. The attendant then carried the body to the mortuary. After Zhang's brother and others examined the body, they observed a straight knife mark and suture marks running from the neck to the lower part of the body, indicating that the entire body had been dissected by the hospital. Zhang's family was deeply saddened by the sight and immediately photographed the body in front of the hospital director as evidence. The body was temporarily placed in the coffin and kept in the mortuary. Zhang's family left the hospital and reported the matter to Deng Zhenquan, commander of the fortress, for investigation.

Statement from the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Traffic Department Workers' Reorganization Committee 112

▲ Denies Anti-Chen Leaflets

The Beijing-Shanghai Railway Traffic Department Workers' Reorganization Committee stated that recently, someone has been distributing leaflets in the name of all colleagues in the Traffic Department, criticizing the newly appointed Chief of the Traffic Department, Chen Chengshi. A meeting was convened on the afternoon of the previous day and it was concluded that the leaflets were actually forged by a small number of people and were not related to the name of all colleagues in the Traffic Department. It was decided to send a letter to the Railway Bureau to investigate the matter thoroughly and issue the following declaration: "Recently, it has been discovered that unscrupulous individuals have been distributing leaflets in the name of the colleagues in the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Traffic Department, fabricating facts and damaging the reputation of Chen Chengshi, Chief of the Traffic Department. This is akin to framing and is like the work of ghosts and goblins. All traffic employees of the entire route are indignant. In addition to issuing a general order to the branch secretaries, team leaders, and all members of the committee to thoroughly investigate the source and report it at any time so that they can be brought to justice and prevent traitors, we are especially afraid that the outside world will not understand the truth and will misunderstand. We hereby declare that the leaflets have nothing to do with all of our traffic employees."

Store Employees Can Join Trade Associations 113

▲Representation Rights Confirmed

▲Old Terms and Conditions Guaranteed

▲No Worries about Improved Treatment

The Shanghai Special Municipality Party Headquarters' Public Training Committee, considering Article 10 of the Implementation Rules of the Trade Association Law, which states, "Each company or firm may send one or two representatives, limited to managers or owners. However, if the average number of store employees in the past year exceeds fifteen, one additional representative may be sent, elected by the store employees," found the meaning of the phrase "one additional" ambiguous. It proposed the following remedial measures: (1) The word "may" in Article 10 of the Implementation Rules of the Trade Association Law, which states, "If the average number of store employees exceeds fifteen, one additional representative 'may' be sent," is vague and ambiguous. It should be submitted to the Legislative Yuan of the National Government for clarification and amendment. (2) If store employees and workers, due to actual needs, request employers to improve treatment, they may jointly petition the local party and government authorities for mediation. (3) All terms and conditions already signed between store employees and workers in various industries and the respective employers shall be reviewed and protected by the local party and government authorities. Those that violate existing laws and regulations shall be jointly ordered to be revoked. The above three points have already been submitted to the Central Party Headquarters for approval and record. Yesterday, the committee received Instruction No. 13225 from the Central Training Department approving the request. The original instruction is recorded as follows: "Received your report. After investigation, the three remedial measures presented, except for points 2 and 3, are approved for record. As for the first point requesting amendment to Article 10 of the Implementation Rules of the Trade Association Law, the Ministry of Industry has already amended it to: 'The representatives of members in Article 7 of this Law shall be one or two representatives from each company or firm, limited to managers or owners. If the average number of store employees in the past year exceeds ten, one additional representative shall be sent, elected by the store employees of the respective company or firm, but not exceeding three in total, excluding branch offices. You are hereby informed. This order.'"

Special News from the Shipping Industry 118

▲Escort Team Has Boarded the Ship Yesterday Shanghai Steamer of the Three Companies has added an escort team. Thirty-two police officers have been recruited, originally intending to send them on board early. Later, due to the Public Security Bureau's failure to issue weapons and the increase in water fees, it caused opposition from all parties and could not be resolved. Recently, Sanbei Zhaoshang Ningshao, etc., believing that the naval police have been recruited and the sea bandits in Zhejiang are unstable, dispatched personnel to each ship yesterday to protect passengers without waiting for the issuance of weapons and the resolution of the fee increase, and urged the Public Security Bureau to issue firearms quickly for transfer to the escort.

▲French Ship "Shangjiang" Had an Accident According to Dalu News, this port received news that the French ship "Fuyuan" (transliteration) was sailing to Chongqing and ran aground and sank on Saturday 80 miles upstream from Yichang, blocking the river. Therefore, all ships going to Chongqing are now docked in Yichang and cannot move forward. It is not yet known whether there were any casualties in the ship's accident.

▲"Changan" Ship Tea Room Beaten Up The Sanbei Company's "Changan" ship returned to Shanghai from Hankou yesterday and immediately set off for the capital. When the ship arrived in Shanghai, its tea room reported to the Seamen's Union that it had been beaten by part of the comprador. It is said that the reason was that on the 17th of this month, when the ship was in Hankou, the comprador Li Changqing gave rewards to the sailors, etc., but did not give them to the tea room. The tea room representatives Zhuo Ciku questioned the comprador, which led to an argument and a conflict. Li Changqing ordered Xi Hui, Qi Abing, etc. to drive the tea room out, which led to a mutual beating. As a result, Zhao Shichun from the tea room was injured and fell into the water. He was later rescued. Zhang Guangcheng, Tang Shougen, Sheng Fusheng, etc. were also beaten and injured. Ren Jinwang, a middle rudder tea room worker, died from excessive fright during the beating. It was not discovered until the 18th, and the Hankou Court was immediately notified for inspection and the injured were sent to the hospital for treatment. The body was coffined by the Sanbei Company. The court is still waiting for the family members of the deceased to appear in court before making a judgment. The tea room workers requested the union to take charge, so it has not yet been resolved. The ship has already gone to Beijing and must wait for its return to Shanghai before negotiations can be held.

Western Businesses Agree that the Public Works Bureau Should Purchase the Dahua Hotel 119

Harris, manager of the Yongming Life Insurance Company in this port, believes that the Dahua Hotel in West Shanghai is scheduled to stop operating the ballroom at the end of March and will be renovated into housing. It is a pity to destroy it because Shanghai lacks gardens and assembly halls. Moreover, the Public Works Bureau's existing buildings will soon be insufficient for office space. He specially wrote to various Western newspapers, advocating that the Public Works Bureau issue public bonds to purchase the property, using the Italian Garden as the city hall and the winter performance venue for the orchestra, and gradually constructing new office buildings on the remaining land, relocating all departments and libraries of the Public Works Bureau, and selling the existing site on Fuzhou Road. With the high land price of Fuzhou Road, if a good price can be obtained, it can not only recover the public bonds, but may even have an extra one or two million taels to cover construction costs. Yesterday, a reporter from the Da Mei Evening News interviewed various key foreign businessmen to ask for their opinions on this plan. They generally expressed their approval, as long as the Public Works Bureau can benefit from it. For example, the Director-General of the Public Works Bureau, Fessenden, said, "This seems to be an excellent plan, as long as the Public Works Bureau can sell its existing site and at the same time purchase the original site of the Dahua Hotel at a fair price." However, if the existing site cannot be sold at a good price, and the Dahua property is rashly purchased and huge sums are spent on building houses, it would be an unwise move. As for the location, it is also very suitable. The municipal government does not necessarily have to be located in the central area. There are many precedents in Western countries. Moreover, the bureau's existing buildings are already narrow and insufficient for office space, and there is a need to expand. Other people, such as Raven of the American Feng Bank, Ward of Huiluo Company, Priest Macbeth, and Ismail, a large restaurant merchant, also had roughly the same opinion.
