(2) For members who have been dismissed by the employer before the expiration of the employment period, a letter will be sent to the trade association to issue a notice ordering each store to resume work as soon as possible to avoid disputes. (3) The issue of severance pay will be resolved by the union convening a representative assembly. The above four motions were passed. ▲Silk Floss Industry Trade Union The preparatory committee held its first preparatory committee meeting on the 18th, chaired by Chen Ziming. After the customary formalities, Chen Ziming was elected as Standing Committee member and Director of the General Affairs Section, Qian Rongfu as Director of the Registration Section, and Fu Decai as Director of the Investigation Section, and then the discussion began and the meeting was adjourned.

High Court Opens Trial to Investigate Hong Shen's Suspected Reactionary Activities 125

▲ Due to a Telegram from the Hankou Headquarters

▲ Hong Voluntarily Surrenders to the Police Station Before Arrest

▲ Hong's Interrogation Process at the Court Yesterday

▲ Allowed Bail After Investigation in Court

▲ Hong Shen Goes to the Police Station to Surrender: Hong Shen (style name Qianzai), professor at Fudan and Jinan Universities, and his friend Tian Han, etc., rented a house in the Weihaiwei area of the International Settlement last August to establish the Modern Arts and Sciences Research Institute. Hong served as the director. Later, the authorities discovered that the institute was organized by reactionaries and notified the Special District Court to close it down to prevent unrest. Half a year passed, and it was thought that no further problems would arise. Unexpectedly, the Staff Office of the Land, Sea, and Air Force Headquarters in Hankou recently discovered that Hong Shen was also a reactionary member of the institute. Since Hong lived in the International Settlement, they should request extradition from the Consular Body. They specially requested the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to handle the matter according to the law. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, considering that there was already a formal court in the International Settlement, could directly conduct the trial. Therefore, it ordered the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court to arrest Hong and interrogate him. Wang Zhennan, the Chief Prosecutor of the High Court's Second Branch, immediately issued an arrest warrant and handed it over to the General Police Station for execution. However, since Hong lived in the French Concession, it could not be directly executed. Hong had already heard about it, so he, along with lawyer Zhan Jifeng, went to the police station to surrender at 2:30 PM the day before yesterday.

▲ First Investigation Court Session: Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Criminal Court of the High Court's Second Branch. Many people were present to observe the proceedings. The initial procedure for this case required investigation, so Chief Prosecutor Wang took the stand for interrogation. Investigation court sessions in ordinary courts are usually not open to the public, but the situation in the International Settlement is different. According to the agreement on the recovery of jurisdiction, investigation court sessions can also be open to the public, and lawyers are allowed to appear in court. However, lawyers can only state opinions and cannot argue. Therefore, Hong's lawyer, Zhan Jifeng, and the police station's lawyer, Gan Jingxian, both appeared in court successively. This was the first time since its establishment that the High Court's Second Branch had held an open investigation court session.

▲ Tian Han Invited Me to Be the Director: According to Hong's confession, Wang Prosecutor interrogated that his ancestral home was Changzhou, he was 38 years old, and he lived on Rue Bourgeois in the French Concession. Regarding the details of the Modern Arts and Sciences Research Institute, allow me to explain in detail. Because I have quite a bit of research in drama and enjoy a little fame in society, schools often invite me to serve as a director or principal. However, I always refuse, except for drama schools, because that is what I like. Tian Han and Ouyang Yuqian are both dramatists and my friends. Ouyang has been hired by Chen Mingshu, the Chairman of the Guangdong Provincial Government, to go to Guangdong to establish a drama research society with an affiliated drama school, and he sent a letter inviting me to be the principal. The following year, Tian Han and his friends wanted to organize the Modern Arts and Sciences Research Institute and asked me to serve as the director to attract attention. Because it was difficult to refuse, I agreed, but I stated that I would not be responsible.

▲ Searched for Three Hours: Tian's finances were quite tight. The equipment in the institute was all borrowed. The rent for the institute was 200 yuan per month, but the institute only allowed 150 yuan. Later, I mediated and agreed on a monthly rent of 160 yuan. The institute's courses were divided into four categories: drama, society, literature, and art. I was in charge of drama, Tian was in charge of literature, Yang Zhiming was in charge of society, and a person named Xu was in charge of art. When school started, surprisingly, not a single person studied drama. I was very disheartened, so I changed to teaching a course on "pronunciation and elocution." However, most students were unwilling to be trained by me, so I only went to the institute two or three times and taught one class. I generally did not inquire about other matters. Later, a student from the Nanguo Drama Society, which was run by Tian Han, was arrested in Nanjing by the Garrison Headquarters. Tian's residence was also in the French Concession of this port. The Garrison Department, together with the French police, sent personnel to Tian's home to search and seized several books and arrested two people. They also came to my house to search. Because I had a lot of books, the search took three hours that day.

▲ The Process of Severing Ties: Later, I submitted a report to the Municipal Party Headquarters, stating that I could not bear criminal responsibility because of friendship. The Municipal Party Headquarters advised me to sever ties with the institute at that time. On October 5th, I followed the advice and resigned from the position of director and also resigned from the professorships at various universities. Later, on October 7th, I published a statement in the newspaper declaring that I would sever ties with the academic world and specialize in screenwriting for the Mingxing Film Company. Later, the institute was closed down by the government due to reactionary activities. Unexpectedly, the landlord actually demanded the rent owed from me. I hired a lawyer to negotiate with the landlord, stating that I had no relationship with the institute and that a contract had been signed by others when renting the house, and there was a legitimate shop guaranteeing it, so they should reason with the guarantor. I only knew a person named Zhu among the staff of the institute, who is now being treated for illness in Hangzhou.

▲ Met with Chen Lifu in Nanjing: Wang Prosecutor asked what the Central Party Headquarters' punishment of you was for. Hong confessed that it was also related to this case. Chen Lifu, the Secretary-General of the Central Party Headquarters, even ordered me to go to Nanjing to inquire in person. So, between December 17th and 18th, I went with Zhu Yingpeng, a supervisor of the Municipal Party Headquarters. After meeting with Mr. Chen, I was treated very favorably. Later, I heard that my punishment had been revoked. The court also asked if the students of the institute said that the researchers in the institute were Marxist. Hong confessed that he did not ask about anything in the institute and knew nothing about it. The court then gave him an English lecture to read and asked if Hong had seen it. Hong confessed that he had never seen it before and claimed that Pan Gongzhan, the director of the Municipal Party Committee and Social Affairs Bureau, could now prove everything about the advice of the Municipal Party Headquarters and the situation of severing ties with the institute.

▲ Pan Gongzhan Testifies in Court: At that time, Director Pan was sitting alone in the audience listening to the trial. Chief Prosecutor Wang immediately ordered the court clerk to ask Pan Gongzhan, the director of the Municipal Government's Social Affairs Bureau, who was sitting in the audience, whether he was willing to testify in the case. Director Pan indicated that he was willing and immediately went to the witness stand to report his name, age, and occupation. Wang Prosecutor then said to Pan, "This court is acting on a document from the Staff Office of the Land, Sea, and Air Force Headquarters in Hankou, forwarded by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, stating that Hong Shen founded the Modern Arts and Sciences Research Institute to secretly train communists. Now, according to Hong Shen's confession, he had already followed the advice of the Municipal Party Headquarters and severed ties with the institute, and he claims that you know the whole story. Can you give a detailed account of what happened?"

▲ Written Advice from the Municipal Party Headquarters: Director Pan immediately stated, "This matter started near the end of last summer vacation, when schools were preparing to open. Because I saw newspaper advertisements for the Modern Arts and Sciences Research Institute, with Hong Shen's name as the director, I had a friendly relationship with Hong and could not bear to see him being used by others. I specially advised him not to take the position of director. At that time, Hong only said that he was helping a friend who strongly urged him, only in name, and not responsible. Later, the Municipal Party Headquarters formally advised him in writing to sever ties with the institute as soon as possible, otherwise, if reactionary actions were found in the institute in the future, the director could not be excused. Hong then accepted the advice and immediately replied to the Municipal Party Headquarters, saying that he had not only resigned from the position of director of the Modern Arts and Sciences Research Institute and severed ties with the institute, but also resigned from the professorships at other schools he held, so as to avoid being suspected of inciting young students. After that, he would specialize in directing movies for the Mingxing Film Company." ▲ The Central Government's Investigation: When I met Hong, I still asked about the content of the research institute and who rented the premises. According to Hong, he had been friends with Tian Han for a long time, and Tian bothered him with the position of director, so he could not refuse to help. However, from beginning to end, he only went to the institute once to teach a class, and after receiving advice, he also suspected that there was another purpose, so he immediately resigned. The Central Party Headquarters' investigation of this matter was actually based on reports received before the institute was sealed. Because the Municipal Party Headquarters had not yet reported to the Central Government about the Municipal Party Headquarters' advice to Hong Shen to sever ties and Hong Shen's acceptance of the advice. Chen Lifu, a comrade of the Secretary of the Central Party Headquarters, wanted to understand the truth of the matter, so he specially invited Hong Shen to Nanjing to inquire about everything in person. Comrades from the Municipal Party Headquarters, in a private capacity, prepared a letter of introduction for Hong and sent a comrade with Hong. Later, according to Hong's return to Shanghai, he had met with important people from the Central Government, and all the suspicions of the Central Government had been understood. This was last month. Hong's departure from the institute was before the institute was sealed. After Hong went to Nanjing to explain, the Municipal Party Headquarters thought that the matter was over.

▲ The Party Headquarters Sends Documents for Reference: Recently, I heard that the court needed Hong to appear in court because of the Ministry's order. Yesterday, I received Hong's words, asking me to testify for him in court and declare the past. So, I advised Hong to surrender, so he surrendered to the police station yesterday. The Party Headquarters feared that the official letter would not be clear enough, so it sent me to listen to the trial in the court and report the process of the case to the court for reference. Wang Prosecutor then asked Director Pan, "What was the reason for the Garrison Headquarters' previous investigation of Hong Shen?" Pan replied, "It was also because of this matter. The Garrison Headquarters sent people to Hong's house to search for three hours." He also asked, "Does the Municipal Party Headquarters have documents to prove the handling of this matter?" Pan said, "I need to check it and follow the court's order to return to the Party Headquarters and order someone to copy a copy of the documents related to this matter and send it to the court for reference."

Hong Shen Granted Bail in Court: Wang Prosecutor then asked Hong Shen whether he had any documents to prove what he had stated to the Central Party Headquarters. Hong confessed that there were no documents. After understanding at that time, Chen Lifu was quite favorable to him. Hong said to this point, and then changed his tone, saying that the court had just instructed that he was handling this case according to a document from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and he had an enemy in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Wang Prosecutor knew that Hong had misunderstood the procedures for handling this case, so he instructed him, "This case originated from the Staff Office of the Land, Sea, and Air Force Headquarters. Because you live in the International Settlement, it was transferred to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and handled through diplomatic channels. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, considering that there are Chinese courts in the International Settlement, did not need to deal with foreigners, so it transferred the order to this court for review. There is no intention. You must not misunderstand. This case still needs to be investigated. You should provide a guarantor and leave to await instructions. Whether or not to prosecute in the future will be officially notified in writing." Hong's lawyer, Zhan Jifeng, had already taken the newspaper with the advertisement about the settlement of the Daguangming case and presented it to the court, and requested Zhou Jianyun, the manager of Mingxing Company, to be Hong's guarantor. Wang Prosecutor immediately approved it and announced the adjournment. It was exactly twelve o'clock.

Wrong Bride Kidnapped 127

▲ Widow Vows Chastity

▲ Neighbor Suffers Loss

A comic kidnapping scene occurred in Yangjiadu, Pudong, the night before last. The bride turned out to be a stranger. The investigation is recorded as follows:

▲ Secretly Planning to Marry a Widow: Tian Guohua, also known as Tian Yangxiao, from Taizhou, is 25 years old and lives in a thatched house at No. 204 behind Yu's Temple in Pudong. He makes a living as a stevedore unloading foreign pine boards. His family is poor, and he has never had a wife. There is a middle-aged widow in the nearby Caonitang area who is slightly attractive. Tian wants to take advantage of her, but he has no opportunity. He secretly conspires with a friend, who designs a plan for him, lobbying the widow's aunt. They agree on a price of 110 yuan, with 60 yuan paid in advance. The deal is settled, and the 60 yuan is paid immediately.

▲ Agreeing to Kidnap the Bride at Dusk: Unexpectedly, the widow learns of this news. Since her husband died not long ago and her mourning clothes have not been removed, she is too sad to do anything else. Therefore, she is determined to remain chaste and vows not to comply. The aunt sees that the matter has reached a stalemate and that the 60 yuan received is difficult to repay, so she agrees with Tian to order the daughter-in-law to get water at the tiger stove on the stone bridge embankment in the East Market of Yangjiadu from 6:00 PM to 7:00 PM the night before last, and Tian will kidnap her to his home for marriage. As planned, Tian is eager to fulfill his dream, but he does not expect to create a comic scene for people to talk about.

▲ Kidnapping Someone Else's Wife by Mistake: The day before yesterday, Tian slightly arranged the room at home, making it look like a new room, and set up a ceremony table outside the room with incense and candles, pretending to be a wedding hall. He also recruited more than ten friends to wait around the tiger stove. However, the widow had been secretly informed in advance and pretended to agree to buy water but did not go. There was a man named Teng Xuezi from Taizhou, who lived in the nearby Laji Hall. He was 34 years old and worked as a clerk in a brewery. His wife, Chen, was one year younger and looked quite similar to the widow. At that time, she was holding a child and happened to be carrying a bucket to buy water at the tiger stove. Tian waited for the widow for a long time but did not see her. When he saw Chen coming, he could not see clearly under the electric light and mistakenly thought that she was the person. He first covered her head with a piece of cloth, called his companions, and they rushed her home. The firecrackers at the door were also set off loudly.

▲ Niece Surrounded: Tian saw that Chen's clothes were old and ordered her to enter the room to bathe and change clothes. Chen was as if she had fallen into a fog and did not understand why. She insisted on refusing to no avail. Because she did not agree to bathe and change clothes, her clothes were torn by Tian. Chen shouted for help, and Tian immediately struck her mouth, causing her to bleed. At that time, Chen's uncle, Han Baxi, happened to pass by the door and saw the incense and candles shining brightly in Tian's house, and the room was noisy. He was curious and went inside to watch. He saw that his niece was surrounded and forced to marry, so he took down Tian's door number and rushed to report to Teng.

▲ Lured into Police Station for Detention: Teng was furious and could not be stopped. He immediately rushed to the First Sub-station of the Third District to file a complaint. The station chief sent police to Tian's house to investigate, but Tian and his gang had already fled. Chen was taken to the station and questioned briefly, and the couple was temporarily released to wait for Tian to be arrested for further verification. After Tian saw someone take away the door number, he realized that he had kidnapped the wrong bride and wanted to regret it, but it was too late. Therefore, he asked a friend to speak to Teng, willing to pay for clothing, medical expenses, and other losses. Teng pretended to agree and instructed Tian to go to the police station to make a statement first. Tian believed it to be true and entered the station, where he was detained. Under the confrontation between the plaintiff and the defendant, the station chief said that the custom of kidnapping a bride hinders the freedom of women and is not allowed by law. Moreover, the person kidnapped was not the person they wanted to kidnap, which is beyond the scope of this crime. He had damaged the reputation of others for no reason, so he ordered the defendant to be detained. Yesterday afternoon, the plaintiff and the defendant were all sent to the Public Security Bureau for questioning.

Feng Bingnan's Opinion on Rickshaw Advertising 130

Mr. Feng Bingnan wrote a letter saying, "Dear Sir, I recently saw a news item about rickshaw advertising in the local section of your newspaper on the 24th of this month, which involves me and does not fully conform to the facts. According to me, although tens of thousands of rickshaw pullers in this port are engaged in humble occupations, they are members of social production, which is no different from those engaged in noble occupations. Moreover, regardless of wind, snow, sunshine, or rain, they run day and night on the road and support themselves. Their perseverance in enduring hardship is beyond our reach. Once they have a disease or are too old to pull a rickshaw, life is even more difficult and miserable. Society should provide subsidies for these people. Therefore, when I donated money to the Rickshaw Gospel Society two years ago, I extracted what I saw and published it in the North China Daily, advocating that advertisements be published on rickshaws themselves, such as wheel covers and the back of the car, and that 10% of the profits be used for relief. The editor of the newspaper specially commented on my proposal and published it in the newspaper to promote social attention. This is the factual process of my proposal to publish advertisements on rickshaws to relieve poor rickshaw pullers. However, the Rickshaw Gospel Society was not initiated by me, and the Baigao Advertising Agency has nothing to do with me, so I must declare the facts to avoid misunderstandings. I hereby inform you and hope that you will check and correct it."

Municipal Public Works Bureau Prepares to Set Up Electrical Standard Clock 131

▲ 15 in South Shanghai... 5 in Zhabei

Last year, the Municipal Public Works Bureau prepared to set up a standard clock in the city, first soliciting prices from various foreign firms, and sending letters to municipal authorities in London, Paris, Berlin, and Tokyo to investigate the style of electric clocks they used and their results. Later, they replied one after another, mostly adopting the same type of heteropolar electric clock produced by the German company Siemens, and the results were good. The standard clock recently installed in the capital is also a Siemens heteropolar electric clock. Therefore, the bureau decided to adopt this electric clock and reported it to the Municipal Government for approval. It is now known that the bureau has signed a contract with Siemens to purchase two master clocks and twenty secondary clocks, which are scheduled to be delivered in mid-June. As for the installation plan, it is said that they plan to install one master clock and fifteen secondary clocks in the South Shanghai District, and one master clock and five secondary clocks in the Zhabei District. The installation location and installation method have been planned, and they can be installed as soon as the goods arrive.

Mud Dredging Begins at South Shanghai Wharf 132

The South Shanghai Wharf in this city is very prone to siltation due to water conditions. During the management of the former Port Affairs Bureau, due to time and budget constraints, the mud dredging of the wharf could not be carried out. After the Municipal Public Works Bureau took over, shipping companies repeatedly requested to deepen the coastline to facilitate the berthing of ships. The bureau also recognized that the siltation of each wharf will lead to abandonment. After discussing with the Public Works Bureau to estimate the project, they prepared to ask the Dredging Bureau to carry out large-scale excavation to achieve a permanent solution. However, Wharf No. 8, rented by Ping'an Company, is particularly shallow, and ships can hardly dock. In order to cope with the emergency, the bureau negotiated with the Public Works Bureau to use its own mud-dredging machine and rent another mud-dredging ship for excavation. It is said that work began the day before yesterday (22nd) and will be completed in about two weeks. The mud dredging of other wharves needs to be negotiated with the Dredging Bureau by the Public Works Bureau.

Wusong Yunzaobang Ferry Increases Ferry Fare 133

There is a commercial ferry at Wusong Yunzaobang, and most of the passengers are workers of Yong'an Yarn Factory who go out early and return late. The round-trip fare has always been 20. Recently, Shen Mao, the owner of the ferry, applied to the Municipal Public Works Bureau to increase the fare because the income was not enough to cover expenses. The workers' round-trip fare would be increased by 5 yuan, making it 30 yuan. Non-worker single passengers would be charged 2 copper coins per trip, as was the case with the ferries of Wusong River. It is said that it has been transferred to the Municipal Government for approval by the Public Works Bureau.

Woman Buys Gold Ring for Two Yuan 136

▲ Discovers It Is a Fake and Is Extremely Regretful

▲ Commits Suicide in Anger

Tang Bangjie, 31, from Danyang, rented a room above a sauce garden shop at 125 Zhiyuan Road, Zhabei. He worked as a noodle cutter at Wufangzhai on Dama Road. His wife, Xi, 26, also from Danyang, has been married for only two years and their relationship is very close. After leaving the shop, she saw a man selling a bright red gold ring on the side of the road for two yuan. She bought it and returned home, feeling happy. That night, when Bangjie returned home, she told her husband about buying the ring. After Tang examined it carefully, he found that it was a fake and scolded her. She was a village girl, and suddenly losing two yuan made her extremely regretful. The next morning, when her husband went out, she secretly committed suicide by taking raw opium. Ma Zhangquan, a Cantonese employee of the Nanyang Tobacco Company, was walking from the company to his residence at No. 43 Qingyun Lane, North Sichuan Road, at 5:00 AM yesterday morning. Ma returned home and told his wife, who was unwilling to lose money for nothing. She reported the matter to the Hongkou Police Station, leading to Chen's arrest. The money he had extorted had been used to buy an iron pot and other items for seven yuan, with eight yuan remaining. Yesterday, he was brought before Judge Feng of the Special District Local Court for interrogation. Chen was found guilty and sentenced to one year of imprisonment. The utensils and the eight yuan obtained through extortion were returned to the plaintiff.

Bride Flees After Six Days 138

▲ Wang Peisheng is Not a Comprador

▲ Ms. Zhu Unwilling to be a Wife

Wang Peisheng, a 30-year-old Suzhou native and leader of the type-setting department at a French newspaper office residing at No. 111 Huanghe Road in the French Concession, married Ms. Zhu, a woman from Zhoupu, on the 8th of this month through matchmakers Ms. Jia Li, Ms. Ni Xu, and Ms. Xu Ni. Ms. Zhu, aged twenty, was described as having bright eyes, white teeth, and fashionable attire. Wang spent a considerable sum, offering full gold and six gifts to secure the marriage. Unexpectedly, only six days after the wedding, on the 14th, Ms. Zhu packed her clothes and disappeared without a trace. Wang immediately went to the original matchmakers and Ms. Zhu's father to demand her return, but Ms. Zhu's father claimed to be unaware of her whereabouts. Later, at around 1:00 AM yesterday morning, Ms. Zhu's father found his daughter at the New Eastern Hotel. All her clothes were gone. He escorted his daughter back to Wang's home, but Wang, distressed by the missing clothes and fearing she would run away again, refused to take her in. He then went to the matchmaker's house in the Nine-Mu-Di area, where he followed Wang and summoned police officer Hou Zhaolin from Precinct 1, Sub-station 19 of the Second District. He had Ms. Zhu and the matchmakers arrested and taken to the police station. Chief Xu interrogated them. Wang stated the above and alleged that they were colluding to orchestrate an escape. According to Ms. Zhu's statement, when the engagement was arranged, the matchmakers said that Wang was a Naimowen (i.e., comprador) and only in his twenties. Now she knew Wang was a type-setter, much older, unattractive, and she did not want to be his wife, and so on. As the case involved criminal matters, it was decided to transfer it to the Public Security Bureau for thorough investigation.

Minutes of the Executive Committee Meeting of the Medical and Pharmaceutical Association 147

The Medical and Pharmaceutical Association of the Republic of China convened a meeting of the Executive Committee at its headquarters the other day. In addition to deciding to invite professors from universities in Guangdong, Beiping, and other provinces to attend and lecture at the general meeting in early April, the committee also discussed the current medical administration. As a result, it was resolved that: (1) Medical administration should also be carried out in two stages: political training and constitutional governance. At present, for already practicing doctors, the authorities should formulate transitional measures, such as provisional regulations. Just as civil servants, lawyers, and accountants have provisional regulations, doctors should also receive the same treatment; (2) The reorganization of medicine and pharmaceuticals should be based on science. Without the promotion of science, there can be no real effect. The association should strongly express its concerns to the authorities. Mr. Yu Yunxiu was asked to draft the proposal.

Copper Man Knows the Time, Fish Goes Abroad Li Xufan 149

My friend Wang Ziyan Chun lived in Beiping for many years. Yesterday he returned to Shanghai and visited me. During our conversation, he mentioned two anecdotes about the old capital's palace, which, though old news, may be unknown to others. I recorded them to share with readers.

▲ The Copper Man of the Imperial Hospital Knows the Time The Imperial Hospital was the Qing Dynasty's national medical institution. Now, only historical records remain. However, two copper men in the hospital still stand majestically. The copper men are purplish-brown in color and about four feet tall. They are naked and remarkably lifelike, representing males. One faces south, and the other stands back-to-back. The front, back, top, and bottom of the bodies are marked with acupuncture points according to the body's blood flow. The two points on the chest are the largest, as thick as writing brushes. There is a hole on the top of the head. When filled with water, water shoots out from the chest points at the change of Zi and Wu (11:00 PM and 11:00 AM). Water also squirts out in turn according to the hours of Chou, Yin, Mao, Chen, etc., daily and accurately. Experts say that these copper men were used to test acupuncture for various diseases. They were created by a famous doctor during the Kangxi period of the Qing Dynasty. It is said that they have been effective for more than 200 years. It is a pity that few modern people know the inner structure and mechanism. It can be seen that ancient people's creations were marvelous and comparable to science. If someone could study them in detail and imitate them according to the method, it might be a contribution to medicine.

▲ Old Fish of Beihai Has Gone Abroad A corner of Beihai (North Sea Park) contains countless fish, and swimming is forbidden. In the past, Emperor Qianlong was a carefree man who often enjoyed fishing there during pleasant weather. He had thin gold plates, about an inch in size, prepared. When he caught a fish, he would engrave the character "One" on a gold plate and attach it before releasing the fish. If the fish was caught a second or third time, a second or third gold plate would be attached. The clanging plates were put back into the middle of the stream. Some fish were caught as many as seven times, and the plates were attached as before. The pond was his pleasure. The Beihai pond has thousands of fish, mostly carp. When the waves are calm and the sun is shining, the red, yellow, black, and white fish leap back and forth, and the surface of the water is brilliant and golden. After the collapse of Qianlong, no one cared about it. When the Republic of China was founded, Feng Guozhang was President and hosted foreign envoys at

Tongue Painting · Cheng · Zhi · Zheng 150

Painters all use brushes. However, some use fingers, which is called finger painting. One out of thousands is able to do it, because his attainment is profound. Recently, a friend told me that a certain person in Beiping is good at tongue painting. He spreads paper on a table, dips his tongue in thick ink, and then applies his tongue to the paper. He paints freely, quickly finishing. When viewed, the paintings of people, landscapes, and flowers are lifelike. According to a certain person, this kind of tongue painting was obtained from a secret transmission. It requires a strong person to learn. When painting, you must put all your strength on the tip of your tongue, which is very prone to dizziness. Before painting, he must drink a cup of wine to invigorate blood. He joined the military when he was young, but now he paints to entertain himself. However, he is getting old and wants to teach someone to prevent this art from being lost.

Beihai. A French envoy was curious and knew the fish's history. He informed the government, which ordered them to find a fish and send it to the Paris Museum. They asked Feng for a large fish with seven gold plates attached to its fins, knowing that it had been caught seven times and was 100 years old. He regarded it as a rare commodity and took many procedures to transport it to Dagukou in a large container filled with water and release it into the ocean. As a result, it was worth 100,000 Chinese coins. Feng happily accepted it. The people of Beiping gave Feng the title of President who Sells Fish.

County Magistrate Kills Thief Record Yun Sun 151

Zhang Yi, the county magistrate of Taixian County, has been in office for six months. His reputation has spread far and wide. He was transferred from Rugao to govern Wuling. He is thirty years old and very capable. He handles everything himself. He often goes in and out of the city streets in plain clothes. On the eve of the Lunar New Year, at three or four in the morning, a thief came to his bedroom and stole two gold watches. Still not satisfied, he then stole the fox fur robe from the outside of the Fushi quilt. Zhang woke up, slightly opening his sleepy eyes. He saw a person standing by the bed in the room. He knew that the person was not a good person and intended to harm him. For self-defense, he grabbed the Browning pistol next to his pillow and killed him with one shot. At dawn, he realized that it was a thief. He immediately ordered the village chiefs to verify the identity of the unknown thief's body. The next day, the case was investigated. The news spread, and everyone said that today's county magistrates are all capable in both literary and military arts. The thief's death was his own fault.

At the same time, it was announced that the head of the Public Security Bureau's family, the prison official's family, and the head of a section of the Public Security Bureau's family had been stolen from. The thief only cares about the administrative officials in a county. Although the thief is dead, he should be a powerful ghost.

Three Hundredth Anniversary of Quinine Lv Bing 152

There is a kind of tree bark in Peru, South America, which is ground into powder and used to treat malaria. It is magically effective. This is the quinine known to ordinary people. The first inventor of the frost was the Countess of Quinine. Therefore, her name is forever associated with the drug. That year, the naturalist Linnaeus named it quinine. According to the time, it is three hundred years from 1931.

Not long after the discovery of the New World, Peru became a Spanish territory. Therefore, among the European countries, the Spanish were the first to use quinine. Later, it spread to England. The society was not familiar with its name, so it was commonly called malaria powder. Later, some shipowners who had sailed to Peru said that the locals called this powder quinine. At that time, the name quinine became very popular. However, the spelling of quinine is the same as the English name for China. Therefore, many people mistakenly thought that the medicine came from the Far East and gave it the alias of Chinese powder. The loss of authenticity from quinine to China is not a joke. Quinine is very effective in the medicine box and benefits the people. The contribution is indeed not small. Therefore, on the 300th anniversary of its invention, I have written it out for the readers.

Nanyang Travelogue (126) Linghua 153

October 1st. Teacher Chen Keyuan invited me to speak on the new Gospel of the world. The next day at 2:00 PM, I took a very small wheel to Gongwenya Port. Mr. Chen Lianqing came to greet me. It was already dusk. I went to his power plant to see its repair equipment. After a while, Liu Zhengchang and Liu Feiran from Pengcheng Company greeted me and stayed at their Hetai store. Feiran had studied at the Military and Political School and was able to handle Chinese affairs. The store was located next to a small river. It was very nice to shower in the river every day. I gradually learned to wear pants and take a bath. But people told me that noon was not suitable. Mostly in the morning and 4:00 PM or late at night.

On the 3rd, I wrote couplets for Pengcheng Company and Duyu School. The couplets read: "Deeply cherish the predecessors and educate the successors" and "Nurture good scholars, beautiful as phoenixes and unicorns, and educate them with a gentle breeze and tender plants."

On the 4th, Chen Lianqing came to talk for another five hours. Chen advocated that the main goal was to widely translate various texts, reprint books and popularize them in various countries. I admired his vision. His ideals and morals are comparable to Zhang Mo Chi, and his scientific and economic ability exceeds his. He argued that industrial distribution could be resolved by citing the Ford Company in the United States as an example, saying that the distribution method between workers and shareholders was very good. The Russians also imitated it. But I asked him, "There are many causes of war. Even if the distribution is fair, conflict is inevitable when males meet. Anarchists do not understand political science. People are political animals, half rational and half irrational. Philosophically, the moral rationality of anarchists is too high. Modern humans cannot understand it. Therefore, the Russian Tolstoyists were eventually swallowed by the Marxist tiger. But its soul is still alive in the tiger's belly. Several Chinese anarchists have joined the Kuomintang. This must be known."

Mr. Chen also recounted a small history of the failure of a new village, which must be recorded. A businessman from Fujian, Chen Yunweng, was sixty years old. He was not well-literate and had made a fortune of more than 100,000 yuan. Suddenly, he lived alone and had a whim. He thought of creating a new village. He hired a secretary to write it into a book, and then had him read it aloud so he could hear it. He printed 1,000 copies, each with more than twenty pages, called Public Life. According to Chen Weng, the method can lead to peace. Even bandits can use it. Therefore, he often thought of returning to his hometown to gather bandits and teach them. He would organize a new community. Lianqing saw his original book on public life and also obtained his revised version, which added up to more than fifty pages.

Old Farmer's Experience Talk Qing Qu 154

Yesterday, an old farmer from a village in the west came to my house. He was over seventy years old, but he was spirited and lean. He was also able to drink heartily. When he spoke, he was like the old days when he hoed the fields. There was no sign of aging. I asked him if this early spring snow, which had not been seen in recent years, would damage the small harvest this year. The old farmer sobbed and said, "This is really heaven. Although there was a snowstorm before the beginning of spring, or it accumulated to several inches, and the ice did not melt, the harm of rice borers and locusts was avoided. The rice can be harvested. This snow is a sign of a good year." "Spring snow is harmful and useless." It is said, "Winter snow is like a quilt, spring snow is like a ghost." It means that wheat values spring snow. It is in the process of development and is destroyed by severe cold. It cannot be compared with the end of winter. I asked him how the broad beans, which are also a major source of small harvests, were affected by the weather. The old farmer said, "Although beans can withstand cold, the damage is even worse than wheat. Asking the reason, he said that wheat, regardless of size, has been diligently cultivated by farmers who have picked up river mud and covered the fields. Therefore, it can reduce the intrusion of cold air into the wheat roots, so it will not die. Once exposed to sunlight, it will flourish as before. It can still be harmless. Otherwise, there will be no wheat rice to eat in April and May. Even if you want to grow a big harvest, you can't. It's not just the villagers who are hungry." He said sadly. He also said that broad beans can still be replanted. If you use a hoe to sow the seeds on the morning of the 13th of the lunar January, they can still germinate and bear fruit in early summer. Otherwise, if you sow the seeds in the afternoon, you will not be able to avoid the wasteland if you want it to grow. Villagers do not know the national calendar, so this is what happened. I asked the old farmer, "If this is the case, even though the weather is bad, human efforts can make up for it. Is it true?" The old farmer said slowly, "I have been working in the fields since I was a child. Now I am old. I don't know how many times I have experienced this heavy snow. Are you suspicious?" However, I am not a farmer, and I still cannot get rid of the feelings in my heart. Therefore, I wrote it down with a pen to wait for those with agricultural knowledge to study it.

Chapter 17: Skillful in Maintaining Youth, Eyebrows Mixed with Green Dai; Unable to Prolong Life, Golden Market with Pricey Horses

A Jin said, No matter what, I won't pawn it for thirty yuan. The head counter clerk said, We say thirty yuan because of the small diamonds around the circle. If there were no diamonds around the circle, we wouldn't even give it that price. You say platinum, we have never heard of platinum. In our pawnshop, no one appraises platinum. No matter how you say it, we only see it as copper. We have to take responsibility. If we pawn fake goods, we have to pay for it. As for gold and silver, we have our own eyes. We don't know what new platinum or black gold is. Pawn it if you want to, or take it back. A Jin felt that the thirty yuan was too far off. If he pawned it back at their price, Miss Sixth would definitely be dissatisfied. He naturally didn't dare to make the decision, so he said, Then let me ask the owner of this watch. It's at this time that their messy hair and simple clothes can show their true colors. Hua Yuanchun glanced at him charmingly and said, Young Master San, you are so powerful. You want to see people's true colors. Then come earlier and come when people haven't gotten up yet. Wouldn't that show their true colors even more? Ye Tonghou shook his head and said, That's called "bed tea". But I never have bed tea in my life. What's the point of that? Too much is as bad as too little. The time in bed is suitable for the first half of the period, not the second half of the period. Just like life in general. The first half of life is always more interesting than the second half.

Finance The Situation of the Gold Market Seems Reversal 156

▲ Banks Absorbing Spot Goods

▲ General Attention Increases

▲ Waves Continue to Be Extremely Fierce Yesterday, February 24th, the gold market tended to reverse, showing signs of rising again, but there were still extreme twists and turns, and it was extremely confusing. The changes ranged from four or five taels to more than ten taels in a short period, which was difficult to predict. Throughout the day, there were actually reversals of twenty-four or five taels, eventually rising by about ten taels. This was mainly because the foreign exchange rate continued to rise by one and a half notches. However, the internal situation was stable in the later stage, appearing wide but actually even. The market transactions varied greatly. In the early market, major players such as Fuchang, Yuanheng, Zhifeng, and Yongshunli bought in large quantities, while Qianchang, Xiangyuan, Mao, Yongtaixing, etc., all sold. The psychology of the industry was hesitant and uncertain. Overseas silver markets reported increases, but they were not affected because of widespread rumors about cash exports, which raised general awareness. The gold price rose as soon as it opened, already breaking through 750 taels. Afterwards, the foreign exchange trend became loose, especially with large households selling off, and rumors circulated internationally about stimulating the silver shortage, so the market turned sharply to a low point. In an instant, a storm occurred, and the price plummeted by a huge amount of twenty taels, suddenly breaking through forty taels. At noon, it rebounded. Those hedging exchange bills and Yuanheng, Fuyu, etc., took advantage of this to buy in, causing it to rise by ten taels. Later in the market, it was heard that a certain bank was buying cash, and exchange bills improved. Buyers on the surface were active. Xietai, Chenfeng, Yongqianchang, Xiang, etc., all brought in goods, so the price soared by more than ten taels, but the state was still uncertain, with fluctuations of four or five taels from time to time. The final count was fifty-seven or eight taels. In summary, the news was complicated, and the control was in the hands of both bulls and bears. For spot goods, an additional five taels must be added. There may be no change in large bars this morning.

▲ A Sudden Collapse in the Middle From the early morning, the April opening price increased by six taels and five qian, to 755 taels. Large bars increased by another sixteen-fifths. The silver price had no fluctuations because of the stimulation of cash activity. Afterwards, there were mutual ups and downs of five taels. Yuanmao Yong and other companies sold, so it dropped to fifty taels. Then, with Fuyu and others buying in, it rose again to fifty-five and a half taels. Zhifeng, Yongchang, Shengyong, and speculators sold out, and it suddenly fell by more than nine taels. The preliminary announcement already showed that English money was up three seven five, U.S. dollars up eight seven five, and Japanese money down four and a half points, so it retreated to fifty taels and five qian, becoming forty-eight taels. However, bank transactions were not forgotten. Taiwan bought May English money at 1275, and Mitsui bought Dalian at one tael, six qian, and six fen. Shortly thereafter, it rose to fifty-one and a half taels. After 9:45, a storm suddenly arose. Various firms, such as Qianchangxiang, Dadecheng, Zhifeng, Shuihongli, Fuyu, and Taixing, enthusiastically sold, especially as English money suddenly turned weak. Banks followed suit and loosened, from 1275 to 13, and the market plummeted by more than twenty taels, to thirty-four and a half taels at 10:45. The market then turned slightly peaceful. After 11:00, Fuchang, Yuanheng, Hengxing, Fuyu, etc., bought in again, while English money (Zhejiang and Jiali etc) absorbed at 129375. After 11:30, it was counted as forty-four and a half taels. Suddenly, hedge funds sold out, retreating to forty taels and five qian, and then retail investors bought in, calculating to forty-four taels. At noon, the market closed at forty-two taels and five qian, and then increased again to forty-four taels. The announced price was changed to 811 taels and eight qian, a decrease of more than sixty taels, and then seventy-seven or eight taels, around seventy taels at noon.

▲ Evening Market Rises Gently The market opened in the afternoon at forty-three and a half taels, then forty-five taels. Indian exchange rates initially fell to three or four annas, then returned to forty-three taels. Soon after, Xieda, Qianchangxiang, etc., chased after purchases, and rumors spread that banks were absorbing spot goods, and English money was also better. Afterwards, the buyers stirred things up, and Chenfengyong, Zhifengyong, and hedgers bought in one after another, and Mitsui and the wheat firms dealt with April English money at 12625, so the gold price gradually rose until it reached fifty-nine taels at 4:00. However, there were four or five taels of intraday trading in between, and it was difficult to handle. Tongtaichang acquired

quite a lot of purchases, and retreated to fifty-five and a half taels at 4:10. At 4:30, the market closed at fifty-seven and a half taels, an increase of nine taels compared to the day before, a reversal of the more than thirty-five taels that had fallen for two consecutive days. The maximum price in one day was fifty-nine taels, and the minimum price was thirty-four and a half taels, a difference of twenty-four and a half taels. ▲ Increase in Handling Fee The Gold Exchange is now planning to increase the handling fee. A notice was issued yesterday stating that starting March 1st, the Exchange will collect a handling fee from both buyers and sellers at the rate of one qian per tael. The broker will receive 75% and the Exchange will receive 25%. The Exchange will then allocate 20% of the 25% commission collected to each broker as an incentive. In addition to notifying each broker by letter, this announcement is being made.

Customer Xian Rice Production Prices Rise Frequently 165

▲ Merchants Have Said They Will Purchase Saigon Rice

Yesterday, customer Xian rice was quite bleak, because after the market opened a few days ago, the market price was unusually high, and customer transportation also felt that the transportation and sale were not cost-effective. The owners believe that there is very little customer Xian rice in Shanghai, and the two major rice producing areas in Jiangxi and Hunan are both disturbed by the Communist bandits, and the existing rice has been robbed. Not only is there no rice exported, but there is also a shortage of food. Therefore, the owners are very firm and unwilling to easily sell. The market is presented as a stalemate. Throughout the market, only the Beiyang Gang did one hundred bags of Jiangxi machine Bian Yuan rice, priced at fourteen yuan. Ganwan and other Xian rice did not have any noticeable transactions. Because the production area market price has been rising, exceeding the sales price in Shanghai, the gang plans to pack the existing rice back. However, because the gold price has fallen back in Saigon and Siam, transportation and sales have gradually become cost-effective. It is heard that some merchants have ordered a batch, and because the rice prices are low in the three northeastern provinces and Korea, they are also throwing the rice to those places for sale.

Distant Months of Wheat Gradually Trending Downward 167

After the market opened yesterday, the prices of distant months of wheat gradually fell, and the market was quite smooth and tired. This was because the gold price was frantically lower, the exchange rate was extended, foreign wheat could be marked, and the weather was very good, and the new wheat was expected to have a bumper harvest. Therefore, factories sold out, and long positions were also sold, and the price gradually fell. There was a slight improvement with short covering before closing. This month is approaching the end-of-month delivery, the factories have received spot, and short covering is strong. Spot wheat arrivals and sales were both lacking. They have not been sold since the market opened.

Sugar Market: Overview of the Sugar Industry Last Year 168

▲ Market Price Fluctuations: Last year, the sugar market began with weakness, then rose, and finally experienced a sudden surge due to increased new taxes, reaching the highest price in years, which was quite astonishing. Tracing back to early spring, the opening price for Dutch sugar, raw sugar, and white sugar was 7 taels and 4 mace. Sales were sluggish, and the market steadily declined, reaching a low of 7 taels. Later, due to the rise in foreign exchange rates, prices gradually increased. However, a decline followed soon after. Subsequently, due to sharp increases in prices in Java and New York, prices rose slightly again, but actual sales remained stagnant, and the market showed signs of hovering. After entering summer, price fluctuations were minimal, but arrivals increased sharply, once dropping below 7 taels before rebounding, reaching a high of 7 taels and 9 mace and 5 fen. After autumn, as planting season approached, prices remained at 8 taels or higher. The price of new goods was above 8 taels. At this time, transactions were frequent, and disposals were often completed. Sales in various places gradually became active, and market sentiment was quite strong, causing prices to rise steadily. Since entering winter, fluctuations have been unpredictable. The current prices for spot raw sugar and white sugar are quite high, with market prices consistently between 7 taels and 6 or 7 mace. Later, upon hearing news of increased tariffs, various parties became active in moving goods, and prices rose to 8 taels and 4 or 5 mace. During the Christmas season, prices suddenly surged, breaking through the 9 tael barrier, reaching a high of 9 taels and 5 mace. Subsequently, with the implementation of the new tariff and the rise in foreign exchange rates, the sugar market experienced a significant upheaval. Market prices soared to 10 taels and 7 mace. Later, as large firms and hoarders took profits, market sentiment suddenly dampened, and prices fell to 10 taels and 2 mace. At the end of the year, with further appreciation of foreign exchange rates and dwindling inventories, the market surged again to nearly 11 taels, and even bids as high as 11 taels and 5 mace were heard. Although no transactions occurred at that price, the trend of rising prices was evident. As for Japanese sugar and other factories, their opening prices were also quite high, and their market fluctuations mirrored those of Dutch sugar, so they will not be described in detail.

▲ Abundant Profits: In the sugar industry, various sectors felt the impact of losses last year and adopted a cautious approach at the beginning of the year. However, although the market price of large shipments saw an increase, it was fleeting, and prices soon declined, causing significant losses. Furthermore, due to tight credit conditions and financial panics, two or three firms were forced out of business. The rumors spread at this time were quite alarming. Fortunately, the situation quickly subsided. The summer saw only mediocre performance. In autumn, there was a slight improvement, but most still suffered losses, primarily due to foreign exchange fluctuations. Since entering winter, actual sales gradually increased, and the market steadily rose. Finally, with the implementation of tariff increases and intensified investigations in various places, prices suddenly soared. Although prices fell back slightly at the end of the year, they eventually surged again, resulting in significant profits. This proved to be the most crucial turning point for the industry, resulting in abundant and impressive profits. Overall, Yuansheng, Yuanhe, Yudateng, and Yuantaiheng each had profits of 100,000 taels. Fangcuihe had 75,000 taels, Fanghuihe and Junyi and Yuanyu each had 60,000 taels, Yiyi had 80,000 taels, Taiji and Maohe had 40,000 taels, Hexing had 20,000 taels, Shouhe had 50,000 taels, Xie'an had 16,000 taels, Zhenghe had 30,000 taels, and Jinyuanxiang had 21,000 taels. The remaining firms each had profits ranging from 10,000 to 30,000 or 40,000 taels.

Youth Forum

Datong University Track and Field Team: South 172

"Study and Sports" is the slogan of our Datong University, and the achievements of Datong University. In a few years, the progress made to such an extent is also based on this.

Since Mr. Shen Kunnan took over as the Director of Physical Education at Datong University, he felt that physical education was somewhat incomplete, because it focused too much on intellectual and moral development, so he vigorously advocated "Sports and Study." The purpose of this was to cultivate a strong body, and then have sufficient energy to study academics and cultivate morality. As a result of Mr. Shen's advocacy, all teachers and students in the school took pride in practicing sports, so the track and field team actually ranked third in the fourth Jiangnan University Games, alongside the Jiaotong University gold standard team of the third Jiangnan University Games. Unexpectedly, the fifth Jiangnan University Games could not satisfy us because of the graduation of old students and the limited qualifications of new students.

Now, because Mr. Shen wants to select real talents in track and field to restore the past honor of our school, he does not select them in one or two days of sports meetings, but often observes and seeks them anytime and anywhere. He has actually discovered a lot of outstanding talents. I might as well make a brief introduction to several people whom Mr. Shen believes have very promising futures.

Li Qiubo is from Xiamen, Fujian. He recently returned from Japan. He and Mr. Nanbu Chuhei, the long jump champion of this Far Eastern Games, are very good friends. Usually, the two of them practice together every day. Their posture is the same, and his result is also outside seven meters, sometimes even overwhelming Nanbu. As for his 100 meters, it is equal to the Japanese Murakami Kunihei's national record of 10.6 seconds. Originally, he was prepared to represent our country in the Far Eastern Games. Unexpectedly, in April last year, when he was jumping in the long jump, he threw his arms back too hard, dislocating the bones of his arms, so he slept for two months. Otherwise, our country would not have failed to such an extent in track and field in the Far Eastern Games. Probably, he will definitely have a very good result for us in the National Games of Double Tenth Festival, and awaken the demoralized sports world in our country.

Gu Yu once represented Jiangsu Province in the National Games. He has won the high jump championship of the Jiangzhe Ten Middle Schools and the sports meeting organized by the Shanghai Western Youth Association. Recently, his result has improved to 1.80 meters, breaking Yu Huaian's national record of 1.754 meters.

He Debao is a famous runner among the Chinese in Shanghai. He has won the Shanghai City Running Championship and represented Shanghai in the National Games.

Xiao Zitong has track and field talent. He is proficient in fifteen sports and has repeatedly won personal championships in various Guangdong sports games. He is really an all-round athlete.

The rest, like Wu Jinqi, Guo Ying, Fang Wenji, and Peng Shuxin, are all athletes who can run and jump well. In short, the current Datong University track and field team is indeed very strong. It is expected that in the sixth Jiangnan University Games two or three months later, and the National Games in October, the track and field team of our Datong University will definitely get considerable results.

Request for Free Education: Huichen 173

Who doesn't know that our hometown, Jiangxi, is a mess caused by the Communist Party? A group of elders are mostly preoccupied with preserving their health and preparing for death, so how can they have the spare capacity to provide tuition fees for their children to continue their studies? But if this is the case, let's drop out of school and go home. No, it's impossible to go home without money. If we don't go home, we still have to ask friends for food expenses in Shanghai. So, what can we, wandering wanderers, do?

But forced by circumstances, we have to seek a way to save ourselves. And "desperation breeds change," there will always be a way to get rid of suffering and trouble. Didn't the Education Department recently request the Ministry of Education to issue a notice to all schools to approve the exemption of tuition and accommodation fees for students from Jiangxi? Isn't this very welcome news? But news is news, and in fact, it is very difficult to achieve the goal. However, partial progress may be easier to achieve results. So, students who agreed with each other, jointly signed a "memorial to the throne." Fortunately, success came quickly, and we received a reply from the school authorities, but it was endorsed with the four words "approved for deferred payment."

"Approved for deferred payment," deferred payment does not require guarantee and interest. This is such a "great kindness," but it is building a high debt platform, and it is difficult to repay when it is heavily accumulated. It is not very cost-effective to owe "debts for the next life." So, some students suggested to continue the "free education movement," and some students also wanted to propose "anti-feeism." In the end, it was decided to mobilize all members to make an expanded petition.

After all, the principal is mostly preoccupied with official documents and rarely in the school or at home. It is especially difficult to go to court to see him. It is better to issue a second ultimatum first, to see if he has any reaction. Otherwise, there are further measures. So, everyone decided to proceed in this way.

Three days after the petition was issued, a note from the Secretariat was placed on Cai's desk. At that time, we were just called back from the reading room by the people in the same room. So, Cai and I were silent in the room for three minutes, discussed a few words privately, and hurried to the call of the Secretary-General. When we were about to enter the door, we saw the Secretary-General sitting arrogantly on the sofa smoking a cigarette. When we stood still to catch our breath, he preemptively asked,

"Isn't this your letter requesting free education?"

"Yes," Cai Jun generously admitted.

"Didn't you say that you have already been exempted from tuition and accommodation fees?" The Secretary also pointed to the list copied from the registration class and asked us again.

"Oh, exempted from fees, what an exaggeration, but how to answer him now?" So, we looked at each other again and thought for a while.

"Exempted, why do you want to ask again?" Then came another round of lightning-fast questioning, so we didn't even have time to answer his second question.

"Because we only saw 'approved for deferred payment, not approved for exemption' on the bulletin board, so we asked again," we finally explained to him in this way. At the same time, we took the opportunity to say goodbye.

Although on the way back, our enthusiasm was blown into coldness by the cold wind, we were still "preoccupied" with the Secretary-General's conversation and expression.

First, the request for free education has been approved.

Second, since it is free, you should not ask again.

In this way, it is no wonder that the Secretary-General is justified and confident. But can the previous resolution of "approved for deferred payment, not approved for exemption" be overturned? Or is it a means of "making the false true and the true false" to deal with poor boys? Or is it a "gold and jade on the outside, but with rotten straw inside" method to avoid precedents? I have always been baffled.

Li Shicen Returns to China: Xu Wancheng 174

Mr. Li Shicen left Shanghai six months ago and went to France by sea. He lived in France and Germany for one year each, and studied music in Germany. He traveled in Europe for nearly three years, passing through France, Belgium, Germany, Poland, and the Soviet Union. He visited the old palace of Louis, searched for the old relics of Napoleon, saw the towering Eiffel Tower, and watched the parallel golden horses. He traveled all over France and Belgium, crossed the Rhine again, listened to the murmur of the water, and mourned the war-torn lands. Berlin is magnificent and Hamburg is prosperous. He has visited all the famous attractions in the German capital. He passed through Poland, stayed for a while, and then arrived in the Soviet Union. He then took the Siberian route and returned to Shanghai last winter.

After returning to China, the philosopher Li will serve as a philosophy professor at Guanghua University this semester, and will also serve as a professor of "Educational Philosophy" and "Modern Philosophy" at the Labor University. Datong University also strongly hired Mr. Li to resume his professorship, and he has already agreed. As for the position of editor-in-chief of the Minduo magazine, he has disengaged from the relationship after the 11th volume of the magazine.

After returning to China, the most urgent thing for Mr. Li is to complete his magnum opus "Philosophy of Life Volume II (Volume I has been published, issued by the Commercial Press, priced at 1.6 yuan), a great book of middle school philosophy.

Mr. Li said that he had traveled to the West for nearly three years, and his life ideas have greatly changed. There are many rare anecdotes about Mr. Li's trip to Europe. I will choose the best to record later, and I will not repeat them for the time being. Now I also heard that the teachers and friends of Datong University and Mr. Li are mostly old friends, and they will initiate a banquet to express their farewell.

Youth Forum Submission Guidelines 175

(1) The text should be about the discussion of youth issues, domestic and foreign studies, or student news notes, school life descriptions, etc., and the style is not limited.

(2) Books are limited to those about youth issues.

(3) Photos are qualified for youth life (such as sports travel, excursions, drama performances, speeches, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth sports, regardless of individuals or groups, are welcome.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) The number of words per article should not exceed 2,000.

(6) Do not write manuscripts horizontally, and do not write in cursive script. Western text can be omitted if possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

Social News

Meningitis: Mi 176

The death of my younger brother

Is traditional Chinese medicine right or Western medicine right?

Can it be prevented?

"Meningitis,"

Uh, what a terrible term. Indeed, the impression it gave me was really too deep. It had given me a blow that I had never experienced in my life. It made me terrified, disappointed, pessimistic, and painful. Because of it, I had insomnia for three or four months intermittently.

This happened in the early spring of the 18th year of the Republic, which happened to be the lunar New Year. Because it was winter vacation, I lived at home. The second day of Renri was my birthday. My family was preparing to celebrate for me, so everyone went to bed very early that night. My younger brother, who was sixteen years old at this time, was very tired because he had been to Jiangwan and the theater during the day, so he went to take a bath by himself, preparing to go to bed. He said he felt a little uncomfortable, had a headache, and needed to apply Ruyi oil. This was very common, so everyone didn't pay attention. Before going to bed, he also said that he would invite me to Xinya tomorrow to have tea and celebrate my birthday. Oh my god, who knew that an unprecedented disaster was about to befall my younger brother?

Suddenly, a terrible cry broke my deep sleep. I ran down from upstairs to my younger brother's bed at an extraordinary speed. Oh no, my younger brother's face had turned ginger yellow, his eyes were fixedly staring upwards, his whole body was convulsing, his neck was straight, lying diagonally on the bed, and he was silently shaken by the trembling hands of the nanny, breathing rapidly and urgently, with almost no body temperature and pulse. I, strangely, was unusually calm, without the slightest panic. I immediately took a box of Zhuge marching powder and kept hitting it into his nose. Sure enough, he sneezed, but the situation still did not change. I only heard a low and long groan. Because there was no ammonia, I used the night pot in the tea room and heated it up, then baked it on his nose. Sure enough, the situation changed suddenly, he struggled and screamed. At this time, the sky was already slightly bright, and my father, mother, and Dr. Tan, who lived next door, were already standing in front of the bed.

When Dr. Tan was taking his pulse, everyone had to stand quietly. The patient's screaming also stopped, his body was still convulsing, and his rapid and urgent breathing was still fierce. I started to feel a little different at this time. Fear had invaded my heart, because Dr. Tan's expression was a bit terrible, which immediately made me feel that my brother's illness was not ordinary.

"Emergency fright, let's get cinnamon first," Dr. Tan ordered.

At this time, the important role was not the sick younger brother, but the father who was the head of our family. Because Dr. Tan said that this was a very serious symptom, and the situation would be determined within six hours. The medicine was available, but the treatment method was unusual. The medicine with the opposite nature to the one just used would be used at the change of pulse color at twelve o'clock. Because the symptoms were too dangerous, it was difficult to guarantee. The father had to sign before he was willing to prescribe the medicine. He also said that there was no other way to go.

Father had always been indecisive, and he was even more panicked at this time, so Dr. Tan's words were ineffective. At eight o'clock, a traditional Chinese medicine doctor was invited, and he ran away without writing a prescription. Then came a Western doctor Chen, after a very long examination, he said, "I'm afraid it will turn into meningitis." (I don't know what symptom he said this was, because I happened to run away at this time, but I remember that he used an electric light to shine the patient's eyes to test its reaction.)

After twelve o'clock, Dr. Tan ran away. Because I had to take care of four young siblings, I also ran away. I can't remember what that afternoon was like, until midnight, everyone knew that there was no way. We had to carry the patient out to the living room. Dr. Tan's words had gradually gained my father's faith at this time, however, it was too late.

It is so sad to watch the situation of a person who is gasping for breath and cannot die. I finally couldn't bear it anymore, I couldn't care about the dignity of the parents anymore, "Carry him to the hospital, it's better to find a way than to wait for death, "I really can't tolerate it anymore, my conscience has urged me to say this.

It was dawn, and an ambulance of the Red Cross brought my poor younger brother to a certain hospital. I advocated going to the Japanese Doctor Fumin Hospital, but the old man (not the father) said that a certain hospital was good, there were very good German doctors there. Naturally, the old man's words must be right, what does the opinion of a child count?

In the afternoon, it was the afternoon of the second day after the onset of the disease, and also the afternoon that the patient had been in the hospital for half a day. When I went to the hospital to see him, it was said that not a single doctor had come, only the head nurse and nurses changed him (the patient) into a hospital gown, recorded his name, etc., and then left, because they said that the patient had come in at ten o'clock, and the doctor's service time had passed. What to do? The illness is critical, can it be extended to tomorrow for diagnosis just by changing into a hospital gown and adding an ice pack to the head? The rules of the hospital are strict. Although it is a first-class single room, only two people are allowed to accompany, and no more people can join in to discuss solutions. The nurses are like tigers, and if you ask one more question, you will be scolded, especially the green-eyed female head nurse, chasing away the people who ask about the illness like a hungry tiger chasing a sheep. There is no way, you can only ask more
